<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由慚羞，第二種防護律儀的因緣：是有慚愧心，才能夠護戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此思故，或因親近惡友，或因煩惱增多，隨所生起惡現行欲，即便慚羞，速能捨離，勿彼令我違越所受，當墮惡趣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有前述之善思常俱行的緣故，當因為親近惡知識，或因境界現前使自己貪瞋癡煩惱增盛，隨所生起惡行的欲望時，能立即感到慚愧羞恥，迅速捨離惡欲，不讓惡欲現行使自己犯戒，導致將來墮到三惡趣。如此迴轉心念，能防止自己不犯戒，保護自己戒行清淨。慚愧心所及時現行是防護律儀的第二個條件。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名，結稱防護律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名防護律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依善思及慚愧的方法，防護自己不犯戒，這即是防護律儀。要防護戒體，第一是要有遠離思與信進念定慧在一起活動而生起的增上善思；第二有慚愧心，由於無始劫來的煩惱習氣，遇緣會現起，不想要持戒，或是受到惡知識的影響，也會使自己不要持戒，要有慚愧心，很快提起正念，一定要防護律儀，才能持戒清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、還引律儀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科還引律儀，有時失去正念而犯戒，犯戒已後自己懇切自責發露懺悔，稱為還引律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若時失念，諸惡現行，即便速疾令念安住，自懇自責，發露所犯，蠲除憂悔，後堅守護所受律儀，是名還引律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有時忘失正念，有犯戒行為現前時，要很快的能令正念現前安住，而且自己懇切責備自己，在佛菩薩面前，或者是同法的比丘、比丘尼面前，發露所犯。這樣不會有憂慮，或是後悔，因為作錯事，心裡總是不安。如果真的已經作錯，趕快懺悔，懺悔以後，還要再發願一定要堅固守護所受的戒，是名還引律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》蠲除憂悔者：憂悔即是惡作異名，一切違犯皆惡作攝。如法發露能令還淨，是名蠲除。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　憂悔是惡作的別名，意指行者厭惡過去所作的事，而生憂悔，憂悔對修行有負面的影響。所有的違犯律儀的行為都會引發惡作心所現行。按照佛所說的儀軌、方法發露懺悔清淨，能蠲除惡作。犯戒作錯了還是可以懺悔的，懺悔即清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在《釋禪波羅蜜》中提到三種懺悔。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、作法懺：依佛制定罪的輕重，而決定在多少個的比丘、比丘尼面前作法懺，或者在一位同梵行者前發露懺悔。一般作法懺裡面，不能懺四重罪。可是《釋禪波羅蜜》提到《最妙初教經》裡面，說作法懺也可以懺悔四重戒，這是比較特別的。《釋禪波羅蜜》說，佛在這一部經裡說，如果犯了四重罪還可以懺悔。對作法懺怎麼懺呢？要請三十位清淨的比丘僧，於大眾中，犯罪的比丘出來發露，然後這三十位大眾僧為他作羯磨成就，這個人這樣作以後，在三寶前作種種的行法，還要誦比丘戒一千遍，可以得到清淨。當然最好他誦完千遍，又能拜佛修取相懺，如果能取得佛菩薩的加持，見光、見花，或作到好的夢等，那是更好，這可以滅罪清淨。大乘經說無生懺可以使四重罪懺悔清淨。作法懺能夠懺除的是障道罪，可是殺生還是要償命，性罪不能懺清淨。障道罪指違背佛制，障礙修學聖道的罪，若修了作法懺，不障礙修學聖道。但是所作的殺、盜、淫、妄等等罪，還是得去受果報的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、觀相懺悔：這是要修禪定，在禪定裡面，懺悔自己的業障，然後見到種種的好相，或是在夢中看到好相。這樣可以說有懺罪清淨的現象。可以說這個罪業已被懺掉了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、觀無生懺：觀這一念心不可得。《普賢觀經》說：「一切業障海，皆由妄想生，若欲懺悔者，端坐念實相；眾罪如霜露，慧日能消除，是故應至心，懺悔六情根」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有情造的惡業像海水一樣那麼廣大、那麼多，而業障海從一念妄想生出來的。要懺悔的人，只要端坐念實相，諸法的實相是空，畢竟空。心也不可得，色也不可得，若能念勝義諦，是無生懺。一切法無生，是說一切法是不真實的，如果能夠通達一切法是不真實的，心與空相應，所有的罪都像霜露一樣，太陽一出來已將它消除了。罪業也是虛妄不真實，為什麼有情會受苦，因為有情執著它是真的，如果得了聖道以後，在受果報時，也不覺得很難過，因為知道一切法是如幻如化的。反之受果報時，依所受果報再起惑造業則是沒完沒了。所以要有至誠心來懺悔自己的六情根。眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意，是六情根。如果成功得聖道，可以將業障連根拔起，一切罪根皆懺悔清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觀這一念心無生時，能了知：「福尚沒有，何況非福？」惡業是非福，是不好的事情，福報尚且不是真實的，何況是這個罪業呢？罪業不真。那怎麼觀這一念心呢？要看看心是不是真實的？心如果真實的在自己的身體裡面，不需要靠六根攀緣色、聲、香、味、觸、法即能生起，應該本來已存在那裡。想一想，自己的心是本來在哪裡？在自己的身體裡面嗎？如果沒有接觸到境界，會不會生起這一念心？如說想吃飯，或想讀書，或想作什麼，都是由境界引起有所造作的想法。所以心不在內。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《摩訶止觀》卷1說：「根塵相對一念心起，能生所生無不即空，妄謂心起。起無自性、無他性、無共性、無無因性；起時不從自他共離來，去時不向東西南北去。此心不在內外二中間，亦不常自有，但有名字名之為心，是字不住亦不不住，不可得故。生即無生，亦無無生，有無俱寂。凡愚謂有，智者知無，如水中月得喜失憂，大人去取都無欣慘。」智者大師說，根塵相對一念心起，能生所生無不即空，心不在內、外、中間，但有名字，名字也不可得。罪從心起，若觀心不可得，心都找不到了何況是罪？罪也就不可得，這稱為「罪從心起將心懺，心若滅時罪亦亡，心亡罪滅兩俱空，是則名為真懺悔。」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　達摩祖師傳法給慧可時，慧可說：「我心不安，老師你替我安心」。達摩祖師要他去找心出來，即可為他安心，結果慧可法師遍尋不著，達摩祖師說：「與汝安心竟」。各位、找找看心在哪裡？靜坐時要想這件事，想到心不可得，罪更是枝末，罪由心所生，如果這樣修到與定心相應，達到無分別智的情況之下，無生懺已成功了。詳細的文還可以去看《釋禪波羅蜜》，裡面很清楚說如何修無生懺。像修第一義諦的四尋思、四如實智，如果真的能夠通達到見道位的話，無生懺已成功了。或是修無我觀，或是修法空觀，這都是端坐念實相，無生懺。這種懺法是根本將罪業都從罪根連根拔起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《勝妙定經》說，直心坐禪是第一懺悔。至於懺悔時，靜坐能懺悔嗎？有的人可以，有的人不行。如果靜坐時，要修止即能修止，要想修觀即能修觀，能夠自在而轉，這時不需要再去拜佛、誦經，可以直接坐禪觀實相。如果坐下來不能，都用不上力，很久都沒有消息，也不能得定，坐下來老是昏沈妄想。這時必須去拜大悲懺，或者是梁皇懺、八十八佛等等，是必須加行了。修不來表示業障太重，沒辦法修觀相懺悔，或是無生懺，會有這樣的情形或這樣的分別。不過，雖然作錯了還是有機會懺悔，但是要多讀經典，才知道怎麼樣懺。犯戒如果懺悔清淨，還能恢復清淨的戒體，這是還引律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、下品律儀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科下品律儀，少分遠離十惡業是下品律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4221"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於殺等諸惡業道，少分遠離，少時遠離，唯自遠離，不勸進他，不以無量門稱揚讚述，亦不見彼諸同法者深心慶悅、多生歡喜，是名下品律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下品的戒是怎麼樣？對於殺生等十惡業道，只有少分的遠離，只能遠離下品的十惡業道；少時的遠離，乃至少到一日一夜，或是半個月，或者一個月，或者是一年，一年以內；只是自己遠離十不善業；並不勸他人不作不殺等的十不善業道；又不用種種的方法來讚歎持戒的功德，看到持戒清淨的同修、同法者，沒有從心裡上很高興的慶賀喜悅，隨喜功德，不能生出歡喜心。這樣的持戒，即是下品律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、中品律儀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科中品律儀，多分持清淨是中品律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於諸惡多分遠離，多時遠離，不至命終，自能遠離，亦勸進他，然於遠離不以無量門稱揚讚述，見同法者不深心慶悅、生大歡喜，是名中品律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　持中品戒的人，可以遠離下品與中品的十惡業道，這是多分遠離。少分是持戒者只能遠離下品的十惡業道，而多分是指遠離下品與中品；在時間上，超過一年以上，都能夠不作這些十惡業，但不是盡形壽持的。自己能夠遠離十惡業道，也勸他人遠離，可是沒有很積極的讚歎持戒的功德；見到有人持戒清淨，也不能隨喜，不能深心慶悅、生大歡喜。這種持戒的心態是屬於中品律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰七、上品律儀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科上品律儀，完全沒有如上所說過失，稱為上品律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於諸惡一切分、一切時自能遠離，亦勸進他，以無量門稱揚讚述，見同法者深心慶悅、生大歡喜，是名上品律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是對於十惡業道，一切的上中下品通通能夠遠離；這裡說的一切時是指盡形壽，持戒者盡形壽都能夠遠離十惡業道；又能勸他人持戒；而且能以種種的方法來讚歎持戒的功德；也能夠隨喜他人持戒清淨，自己生大歡喜，能有這種品德和特性的人，持的是上品戒了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰八、清淨律儀2　巳一、靜慮攝2　午一、辨相2　未一、舉初靜慮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科清淨律儀，禪定能夠損伏煩惱，令心清淨，而不犯戒，因此禪定能使律儀清淨，這是定共戒。靜慮律儀也就是定共戒，分二科；第一科靜慮攝，說明世間靜慮，又分二科；第一科辨相，辨別世間靜慮相，又分二科；第一科舉初靜慮，舉初禪為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="14978:40982"></a>若即於此所受律儀能無闕犯以為依止，修無悔等乃至具足入初靜慮，由奢摩他能損伏力，損伏一切犯戒種子，是名靜慮律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若對於所受的戒能夠不犯四重罪，也不犯輕罪，內心沒有憂悔，心裡安定、快樂，依此戒清淨的力量修禪定，乃至成就初禪，成就初禪之後，由禪定的力量能損伏一切犯戒種子，稱為清淨律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　具足入初靜慮是指行者修初禪圓滿，具足初禪的尋、伺、喜、樂、心一境性五法。靜慮律儀也就是定共戒，為何稱為定共戒？得了禪定時，一定自然遠離十惡業，內心清淨，戒就清淨，戒隨定心轉。當然最好是不要犯戒，犯了戒修行聖道有很多障礙。生活中也有很多的憂悔，憂悔則不能得禪定，因此持戒不清淨的人，不能得禪定，因為修定時，以前作過的壞事，或是犯戒的事，都出現，能障礙得禪定。如果障礙常常出現，要怎麼辦呢？彌勒菩薩說沒關係，只要繼續修，繼續跟它鬥戰，總有一日還是會戰勝的。當然彌勒菩薩說要懺悔，可是懺悔了，障礙仍然現前，那是因為還沒有作到無生懺以前，不可能將犯戒種子斷除，它的影像會再出現，則不能得定。但是彌勒菩薩說沒有關係，繼續跟它戰鬥，最後正法一定會贏，即是要持續不斷努力。〈聲聞地〉也說過，當然是無生懺才能夠贏過它。一定要努力，不要想無生懺不可能，至少取相懺也要得到，不然最少要作法懺，向清淨的比丘、比丘尼發露懺悔，以後不要再作了，一定要發願，不要再作。論上很注重發願，發願才會得到戒體。非常有用，願力非常重要。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《釋禪波羅蜜》提到十種持戒：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一持不闕戒，是指不犯四重戒的殺、盜、淫、妄。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二持不破戒，不犯中品戒，不犯中品罪。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三持不穿戒，不犯下品戒，不犯比較小的罪。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四持無瑕戒，不起諂心與種種煩惱尋伺，就是不能雜念，這是定共戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五持道共戒，道共戒又稱為持隨道戒，是證初果時成就的無漏道共戒，下面會說到道共戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六持無著戒，三果以上的聖人才能持無著戒，三果斷欲界九品修惑所持的戒，也名斷律儀戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七持智所讚戒，智慧的人所讚歎的戒，即是大菩薩所持守的戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八持自在戒，是菩薩持戒於種種破戒緣中，而得自在。可說菩薩知罪不罪，不可得故，但隨利益眾生而持戒，心無所執，這是自在戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九持具足戒，菩薩能具一切眾生戒法及色地戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十持隨定戒，不起滅定，現種種威儀戒法，以度眾生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是《釋禪波羅蜜》說到持戒共有十種。前四種是世間的清淨戒，是通向出世間的基礎；第五種與第六種，是出世間清淨的戒。第七種到第八種，是出世間上品又上品的戒，因為是菩薩才能作到這些。凡夫菩薩只是學習而已，還不能得到真正的智所讚戒、自在戒、具足戒、隨定戒。經典上說，只有佛一人能夠持淨戒。為什麼要持戒呢？因為戒如果沒有清淨，不能得定，所以勸大家一定要持戒清淨。但是萬一不小心犯戒，文中提供三種方法，一種是作法懺，一種是取相懺，一種是無生懺。其中最鼓勵無生懺。而如果無生懺修不起來，要先懺悔，是作法懺或拜大悲懺，或者三千懺等，懺悔業障後，再來修無生懺。最重要是要得到無漏慧，才能夠真的罪業消除。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《華嚴經》說，發心畢竟二不別，初發心和究竟不二，那是利根的菩薩才可能作到；他一發心受戒，馬上所有的戒都圓滿了。這種是利根菩薩。《釋禪波羅蜜》又說到破戒有四種情況：一、破戒但可以得禪定；二、破戒不能得禪定。三、不論破戒或持戒，都不能得禪定。四、另外有一種人，不論戒或者持戒，都得禪定。為什麼破戒能得禪定呢？因為前一生的定修得很深，已經栽培了強大的定善根，定的功夫很深，這一生只要一用力，禪定會重新現前，這是前生定功栽培深厚的緣故。因為定的力量大，大過破戒的力量，雖然破戒，只要有一點悔過的心，定是可以生起。破戒還能夠有禪定，這是特別的情況。當然持戒清淨比較容易得定。有的人持戒也不能得定，是由於前生修定的善根不夠，或者很慢很慢，才能夠得定。總之一般人一定要持戒清淨才能得到定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》修無悔等乃至具足入初靜慮者：聲聞地說：先於尸羅善清淨故，便無憂悔；無憂悔故，歡喜安樂；由有樂故，心得正定。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/28.htm#40983:23206">陵本二十八卷二頁2327</a>）此中等言，等取歡喜安樂應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈聲聞地〉卷28，940頁說：修行人首先要持戒清淨，內心就不會憂愁後悔；由於心不憂悔，感覺歡喜身心安樂；由於身心安樂，能成就正定。此處「等」言，等取歡喜安樂應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例餘靜慮2　申一、例同</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘靜慮，如初禪能有清淨律儀，其餘諸禪也一樣，分二科；第一科例同，即第二、三、四禪也是如此。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4222"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如初靜慮，如是第二、第三、第四靜慮，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如初禪有清淨律儀，如是第二、三、四禪也有清淨律儀的定共戒，也可以稱為靜慮律儀。有的地方說無色界沒有律儀，為什麼？無色界離欲界太遠了又無色身，不需要這些對治，故不建立無色界律儀。有部說，無色界天的人，只有道共戒，沒有定共戒。因為無色有情不需要對治欲的煩惱，這裡只說到四禪，沒有說到四空定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、顯別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯別，顯差別是指與前面所說的下中上品不同，前面的下中上品還是屬於欲界的情況。這裡的清淨律儀，有遠分對治的定共戒，能使令有情遠離惡戒的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中差別者，由遠分對治所攝奢摩他道轉深，損伏惡戒種子。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡的差別是屬於遠分對治，得到禪定以後，定力轉深，能夠損伏惡戒種子，但不能斷除惡戒的種子。對治有四種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、厭患對治，在聽聞佛法與思惟佛法時，以聞思對治惡戒種子，用的是厭患對治。這是一種對治修。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、遠分對治，是世間的修道，得到禪定以後，能夠遠離惡戒種子，只是遠離而已，沒有根本斷除。只是如石壓草，暫時壓住，不讓它起來，遠離犯戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、斷對治，是出世間道，證得第一義諦後，才能夠斷除犯戒種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、持對治，得到無漏定，轉依以後，有無漏的道共戒，能夠任運持戒清淨，這是後得智的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡的清淨律儀，有遠分對治的定共戒，是能夠使行者遠離惡戒的種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名，總結清淨律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此名初清淨力所引清淨律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道，這是最初由禪定的清淨力，所引發的清淨律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、無漏攝2　午一、出聖愛2　未一、辨相2　申一、顯不還果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無漏攝，是聖人所持守的律儀，分二科；第一科出聖愛，又稱為聖所愛戒，又分二科；第一科辨相，辨識其相，又分二科；第一科顯不還果，顯示得不還果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若即於此尸羅律儀無有闕犯，又復依止靜慮律儀，入諦現觀，得不還果，爾時一切惡戒種子皆悉永害。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是修行人對於戒沒有闕犯，不犯四重戒，其他下品的也沒有犯，又有禪定，如果依四靜慮，證入四聖諦的現量覺慧，這時得到三果，無漏聖道的力量令一切惡戒種子全部斷除。前面讀過，如果得到初禪以上，在初禪以上修我空觀，可以一下得到三果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、顯預流果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯預流果，說明初果的道共戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="6471:40994"></a>若依未至定證得初果，爾時一切能往惡趣惡戒種子皆悉永害。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是依未到地定而證得初果，那時往三惡道的惡戒種子，都能夠永遠斷除。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名，無漏的道共戒是名聖所愛戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4223"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此即名為聖所愛戒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初果以上證得無漏聖道時，不會再往三惡趣去，稱為聖所愛戒。我們曾說過，有一個獵人，在森林裡面已經將獵具都佈置好了，準備捉那些動物，可是在回家時，佛陀知道他應該得度了，就去為他說法，說法以後，他得到聖道了。因為他得了聖道，他的心裡已沒有往惡趣的種子，惡戒的種子斷除了，使他的殺生業道無表不生，沒有這種殺生業道的惡戒種子，也不會墮入三惡道了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯無漏2　未一、標名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯無漏，說明無漏律儀，分二科；第一科標名，標出名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此名第二清淨力所引清淨律儀，即此亦名無漏律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道，這是第二種清淨力所引發的清淨慮儀，也就是無漏律儀，或是道共戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、辨相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨相，辨明阿羅漢果的無漏律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此無漏律儀，若得阿羅漢果時，但由能治清淨勝故勝，不由所治斷勝故勝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從初果到四果阿羅漢，都可以有無漏律儀。如果得到阿羅漢果，是由於他的心是清淨的，不是由於他所斷的煩惱很多，而說他很殊勝。為什麼？因為阿羅漢所有三界的愛見煩惱種子都已經斷除，內心很清淨而殊勝，能治的心完全清淨了，不是以所治惡戒種子斷了來說他殊勝。如果初果、二果、三果就不一樣了，二果斷的惡戒種子比初果的多，三果的比二果多，可是四果不用比，因為已經沒有惡戒種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此無漏律儀等者：此顯無漏律儀說名清淨，有二差別。前說得不還果，永害一切惡戒種子；或得初果，永害一切能往惡趣惡戒種子；此由所治法斷而得清淨，於戒律儀名之為勝。今說阿羅漢果諸漏永盡，更無所斷，是故不由所治斷勝，但由彼能治道最極清淨，於戒律儀名之為勝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上內容說明無漏律儀名清淨，有二種差別。前面說得不還果，能永遠斷除一切惡戒種子；或得初果能斷往三惡趣的種子，這是根據所斷除惡法種子，成就清淨的聖道果，在戒律儀中是屬於無漏清淨的道共戒，由所對治的煩惱斷除而得清淨，因此說這些聖人持戒殊勝。現在說阿羅漢將三界的愛見煩惱都已斷除，不需要再斷什麼惡戒的種子。不從他所斷除的惡戒種子來說他的殊勝，而是由他的心達到最究竟清淨的狀態，說阿羅漢的戒律最極殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無漏律儀有二種差別，一種是初果到三果的聖人，另一種是最高果位阿羅漢的聖人。初果到三果的聖人，受持的清淨律儀是很殊勝，原因是所斷除的惡戒的種子愈來愈多。初果斷了往三惡趣的惡趣種子，二果更細，三果斷的更多。到了四果，已完全斷除愛見煩惱，能斷的心清淨了，而說他受持的淨戒最殊勝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、料簡2　辰一、總標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科料簡，再詳細思惟簡別，分二科；第一科總標列，總相標出，將八種律儀歸納成三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是八種總立唯三。一、受律儀，二、持律儀，三、清淨律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這八種律儀全部歸納起來只有三種。一、受戒律儀；二、持戒律儀；三、清淨的戒律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、別配屬</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配屬，將八種律儀各別配合三種律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前二是受，防護、還引是持，下中上三通受、持二，靜慮、無漏是清淨攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前二種能起律儀及攝受律儀是屬於受律儀；防護律儀，與還引律儀是持律儀。下品、中品、和上品，這三種律儀，通於受律儀和持律儀，因為受戒也有下品、中品、上品；持戒也可分下品、中品、上品，所以下中上三品是通於受戒跟持戒這二種；靜慮律儀和無漏律儀，都屬於清淨律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、總決擇2　卯一、明建立2　辰一、辨三種2　巳一、建立因緣2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科總決擇，將所有的律儀作一個總決擇，分二科；第一科明建立，說明建立比丘戒、五戒及八關齋戒的因緣及內容，又分二科；第一科辨三種，分別三種戒，又分二科；第一科建立因緣，說明建立三種戒的三個原因，又分二科，第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4224"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故世尊建立苾芻、近事、近住三種律儀？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：世尊為什麼要建立比丘戒、近事戒（五戒）、近住戒（八關齋戒），這三種律儀呢？近事律儀又稱為近事擁護，是在家菩薩的五戒。五戒弟子要親近善法，承事諸佛菩薩，承事諸善士，由此可以防身語的過失，這是近事戒。近住律儀是指八關齋戒，意指親近三寶、阿羅漢而住，可以防護身語意的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答2　未一、標因</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標因，標出三種因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由三因故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：因為有三種原因，而建立這三種戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、顯義2　申一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯義，顯示三種律儀的意義，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂佛所化有三種類，或有能行離惡行行及離欲行；或有能行離惡行行，非離欲行；或不能行離惡行行及離欲行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛所教化的有情有三種類型；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人能夠遠離十不善業道的惡行，又能修離男女欲的梵行，佛為這種人建立出家的比丘戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人能遠離十不善業，但不能離欲，還是要有夫妻的生活，佛為這種人建立五戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，不能盡形壽的遠離十惡業道與離欲，佛為這種人建立八關齋戒，令他短時期的離十惡行及離欲行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能行離惡行行等者：離十不善業道諸所有行，是名離惡行行。遠離受用欲塵諸所有行，名離欲行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能離殺、盜、淫、妄語等等十不善業道，是離惡行行。遠離受用色聲香味觸男女欲，名離欲行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、配屬3　酉一、苾芻律儀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配屬，將所度化有情的種類與三種律儀配合起來解釋，分三科；第一科苾芻律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依初所化類，建立苾芻律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依第一種所化的有情，盡形壽能離十惡行、也能離欲的人，建立比丘戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、近事律儀3　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科近事律儀，說明近事律儀，分三科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依第二所化類，建立近事律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依第二種所化的有情，盡形壽能遠離十惡行，但不能離欲行的人，建立在家五戒的近事律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4225"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">非居家迫迮，現處塵俗，而能一向相續圓滿護眾學處。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在家人的生活環境複雜，有諸多因緣牽絆壓迫，時時處在充滿色聲香味觸男女欲塵中，不能一向、相續、圓滿地保護、受持眾多的律儀。佛憐憫他們的處境，為他們安立能夠做得到的近事律儀，使令他們能栽培善根，修學聖道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、近住律儀3　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科近住律儀，分三科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依第三所化類，建立近住律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依第三種所化的有情，不能盡形壽離十惡行，也不能盡形壽的離欲，建立八關齋戒，使其短時間內離十惡行和離欲行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣安立呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、釋2　亥一、總顯義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋其中的道理，分二科；第一科總顯義，總相顯示義理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由此不能究竟行俱離行，但當勸進攝受二因，勿彼自謂重擔所鎮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於這類所化的有情不能究竟離惡及離欲，但應當勸化他們短時間的離惡行及離欲行，以栽培善法種子，又不會令他們覺得有太大壓力或負擔很大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、別配支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配支，八關齋戒與離惡行及離欲行的配合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂前三支修離惡行，其後四支修離欲行，離非梵行俱修二種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八關齋戒中前三支，不殺生、不偷盜、不妄語屬於離惡行，後四支的不飲酒、不歌舞伎樂塗冠香鬘、不坐高廣大床、及不非時食屬於離欲行，不淫則是離惡行又是離欲行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4226"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂前三支修離惡行等者：近住律儀，略有八支應修遠離。一、於損害他命，二、於損害他財，三、於非梵行，四、於妄語，五、於酒放逸處，六、於歌舞伎樂塗冠香鬘，七、於昇高大床，八、於非時飲食。今於前四，除非梵行，增離妄語，名前三支離惡行攝。遠離酒放逸處、歌舞伎樂塗冠香鬘、昇高大床，名後四支離欲行攝。離非梵行，由不染習他妻妾故，不損害他離惡行攝；由不染習自妻妾故，不自損害離欲行攝；由是說言俱修二種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　近住律儀的八關齋戒，要略來說有八支應修遠離。一、不殺生是不損害他命；二、 不偷盜是不損害他財；三、不淫是離非梵行，四、不妄語是不說謊言；五、不飲酒是不處於飲酒放逸處；六、不歌舞伎樂塗冠香鬘；七、不坐臥高廣大床；八、不非時食（持過午不食）。其中前四支，除了非梵行以外，是不殺生、不偷盜、不妄語，這三支是屬於離惡行。後四支的不飲酒放逸、不歌舞伎樂塗冠香鬘、不昇高大床，是屬於離欲行。離非梵行是不淫戒，由於不染污習近他人的妻妾，不損害其他有情，屬於離惡行；由於不染污習近自己的妻妾之故，對於自己的離欲行無所損害，因此說不淫戒包括離惡行及離欲行二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、支攝差別2　午一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科支攝差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="49360:41037"></a>問：苾芻、近事、近住律儀，當知各由幾支所攝？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：苾芻律儀、近事律儀、及近住律儀等的主要內涵，各由幾支所攝？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、答3　未一、苾芻律儀4　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，分三科；第一科苾芻律儀，說明比丘戒，又分四科；第一科標，標出比丘戒四支所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：苾芻律儀四支所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：苾芻律儀的內容可以歸納成四部分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為四？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪四種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出四支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、受具足支，二、受隨法學處支，三、隨護他心支，四、隨護如所受學處支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、受具足支，是最初發心受比丘戒；二、受隨法學處支，受戒之後，領受學習戒律中所有與比丘戒有關的事行；三、隨護他心支：避免他人的譏嫌，護持比丘戒必須做到軌範具足、所行具足；四、隨護如所受學處支：對於犯微小罪，能見怖畏，因此而不違犯，或是犯戒後能懺悔清淨，就是能隨順、護持比丘所受的戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4227"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、釋4　酉一、受具足支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科受具足支，說明受具足戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若作表白第四羯磨，及略攝受隨麤學處，是名受具足支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受比丘戒時，作單白三羯磨竟就得比丘戒。羯磨是僧眾辦理僧事的方法，此處是指一般受比丘戒的過程，也就是開會令眾僧一致同意此人受比丘戒；先作一宣白，再作三次宣讀，每讀一次，即於眾中作一次徵求同意，如果一白三羯磨了，眾僧中默然者，即表示沒有異議，而宣佈羯磨如法，議案成立，一致通過。此人就是比丘了。隨學粗顯的學處，以遠離身語不善業道，這是受具足支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》及略攝受隨麤學處者：遠離身語不善業道，是名隨麤學處，身語二業相麤顯故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠離身三的殺、盜、淫，以及語四的妄言、惡口、兩舌、綺語等不善業道，這是隨學麤顯的學處，因為身語二業的相貌麤淺而明顯。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由具此支故，名初苾芻具苾芻戒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於受戒及遠離身語不善業道，受具足戒是成為一位比丘最初的條件。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、受隨法學處支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科受隨法學處支，受戒以後要學戒，除了比丘250條戒，其它由戒引發的相關事行，也都必須學習守護。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自此以後，於毗奈耶別解脫中所有隨順苾芻尸羅，若彼所引眾多學處，於彼一切守護奉行，由此得名守護別解脫律儀者，是名受隨法學處支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從受完比丘戒之後，律藏別解脫戒中，所有隨順比丘戒，或與比丘戒有關的諸多應該學習的事行，都要守護奉行，若能做到，就是能守護別解脫律儀戒的人，這就是受隨法學處支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、隨護他心支2　戌一、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨護他心支，分二科；第一科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由成就此二支者所有軌範具足、所行具足，是名隨護他心支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　比丘成就受具足支及受隨法學處支之後，還必須做到軌範具足及所行具足；包括在僧團裡搭衣、吃飯、靜坐、經行、奉事師長等，所有軌則規範要遵守。所行具足是外出托缽乞食時，要密護根門，不該見聞的不見聞，不該去的場所，如唱令家、婬女家、酤酒家、國王家、旃荼羅羯恥那家都不要去，做好軌範具足和所行具足，可以避免他人對比丘的譏嫌，這就是隨護他心支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、指</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科指，指出如〈聲聞地〉已說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">軌範具足、所行具足，如聲聞地已說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　軌範具足和所行具足在〈聲聞地〉卷22，791~795頁已說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4228"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、隨護如所受學支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科隨護如所受學支，說明比丘若能於微小罪見大怖畏，即能不犯戒，或犯了戒能立刻依法懺悔清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於微細罪中深見怖畏，於所受學諸學處中能不毀犯；設犯能出，謂由深見怖畏及聰叡故；是名隨護如所受學處支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　比丘若能對於微細的罪過，看到很大的過失，因而深感恐怖畏懼，這樣能令他對於所受的戒，保持清淨不犯。假設一時失去正念而犯了戒，也能立刻如法懺悔清淨；由於比丘對犯微小罪見大怖畏，一定能輕重等持；又由於他的聰明叡智，使令若一時失誤犯戒後，立刻對治懺悔清淨，這就是隨護如所受學處支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、近事律儀4　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科近事律儀，說明在家居士五戒的內涵，分四科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">近事律儀由三支所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　近事律儀，五戒的內容可以含攝為三支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為三？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三支？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出三支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、受遠離最勝損他事支，二、違越所受重修行支，三、不越所受支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　近事律儀分成三支：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、受遠離最勝損他事支，就是不殺生、不偷盜、不邪淫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、違越所受重修行支，就是不妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、不越所受支，就是不飲酒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》違越所受重修行支者：謂若違越所受修離欲行，應如所犯發露悔除，是故施設遠離妄語。由有妄語，則不堪任發露所犯，重更修行故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果違越了所受的修離欲行，應該如所犯的戒，發露悔除，不可以遮蓋、覆藏罪過，要對同法者前，依法發露懺悔清淨，因此施設遠離妄語：不妄語戒。若不承認自己有錯，就是犯了不妄語戒，不但沒能完成發露懺悔，而且不能再修行以前所受的不殺生、不偷盜、不邪淫的戒行，所以這一支不妄語戒，就是違越所受重修行支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　犯戒必須重新改過，修正的條件就是不可以妄語。如果一個人說謊話，不肯認錯，他是不會改過的，知道錯承認錯才會改。如果不知道錯不承認錯，就很難改過向善，所以這個不妄語戒也是很重要，這是第二支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、釋3　酉一、初支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋三支，分三科；第一科初支，說明第一支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若永遠離損害他命、損壞他財、損他妻妾，是名初支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　永遠遠離損害他命，就是不殺生；遠離損壞他財，就是不偷盜；遠離損害他妻妾就是不邪淫，這是近事律儀三支中的第一支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、第二支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二支，說明第二支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4229"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">遠離妄語，是第二支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠離妄語是不妄語，這是第二支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、第三支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三支，說明第三支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">遠離諸酒眾放逸處，是第三支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠離諸酒眾放逸處，就是不飲酒，這是第三支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、近住律儀4　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科近住律儀，說明八關齋戒，分四科；第一科標，先標出八關齋戒五支所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="35195:41075"></a>略說近住律儀由五支所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略來說近住律儀，含攝了五支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為五？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪五支呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出五支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、受遠離損害他支，二、受遠離損害自他支，三、違越所受重修行支，四、不越所受正念住支，五、不壞正念支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八關齋戒分有五支：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一支遠離損害他支，就是不損害他人的生命及財產，包括遠離損害他命的不殺生，以及遠離損壞他財的不偷盜。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二支受遠離損害自他支，是離非梵行的離欲行。不只離邪淫，連正淫也不可以。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三支違越所受重修行支，是不妄語。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四支不越所受正念住支，是不歌舞倡妓、不坐高廣大床，以及過午不食。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五支不壞正念支，就是不飲酒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、釋5　酉一、初支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋遠離損害他支，分五科；第一科初支，說明第一支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若能遠離損害他命、損壞他財，是名初支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能離損害他人的生命就是不殺生；遠離損壞他人的財物，就是不偷盜，這是八關齋戒的第一支，不損害他人的生命及財產。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、第二支3　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二支，說明第二支，分三科；第一科標，標出離非梵行，是第二支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4230"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">離非梵行，是第二支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　離非梵行是不淫，這是第二支受遠離損害自他支。離欲的人既不損他，也不害已。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由離此者，不染習自妻妾故，不自損害；亦不染習他妻妾故，不損害他。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於離非梵行，而不染污習近自己的妻妾，即是不損害自己的離欲行，又不染污習近他人的妻妾，是不損害他。這樣的離非梵行，是遠離損害自他支，是第二支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、第三支</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三支，說明第三支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">遠離妄語，是第三支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠離妄語：不妄語，是屬於第三支，這是遠離所受重修行支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、第四支3　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科第四支，說明第四支，分三科；第一科標，標出第四支的內容。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">除離諸酒眾放逸處，離餘三處，是第四支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四支是不越所受正念住支，除了不喝酒以外，其他的三條戒，不歌舞妓樂、不塗冠香鬘、不昇高大床、與不非時食，都屬於第四支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4231"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由歌舞妓樂塗冠香鬘、昇高大床、非時飲食常所串習，若遠離彼，數數自憶：我今安住決定齋戒，於一切時堅守正念。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在家人由於生活所須常常要香鬘塗冠，以香油塗身及唱歌跳舞自娛，坐臥高廣大床，下午喝下午茶，晚上還要全家共聚晚餐。對居士們來說，這是他們日常生活中習以為常的事。受了八關齋戒，必須遠離這些事情，要不斷的提醒自己，已經受了八關齋戒，今日一定要受持守護。所以受八關齋戒的居士最好不要回家，住在寺廟裡。如果受八關齋戒還回家，實在有一點不可靠，回家染污因緣太多，不容易守持。以前佛規定要近阿羅漢住，要到寺廟裡來住，才比較如法。因為寺廟裡沒有歌舞妓樂等可以讓他接觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、第五支3　戌一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科第五支，說明第五支，分三科；第一科標，標出不飲酒是第五支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">遠離諸酒眾放逸處，是第五支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　飲酒能使人亂性而放逸，易令人有邪思惟、邪尋思、及邪戲論，不飲酒是第五支。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼雖安住正憶念支，謂我今住決定齋戒。若為諸酒所醉，便發狂亂，不自在轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就算有正念，知道自己現在正受持八關齋戒，一定要守住八關齋戒。可是如果喝了酒，心神容易瘋狂散亂，不能控制自己。這個大家很容易明白，喝醉酒很難控制自己，這是第五支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八關齋戒中的不殺生、不偷盜是第一支。離非梵行是第二支，不妄語是第三支。第四支是不歌舞倡妓、不昇高大床、不非時食。第五支是不飲酒。八關齋戒又可以收攝成這五支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一支遠離損害他支，就是不侵損他人的生命及財物，因為生命是人活下去的根本，財物是資助生命的必需品，即然每個眾生都貪生怕死，珍惜生命，就不應該傷害眾生的生命，劫奪眾生的財物，所以最先安立不殺生、不偷盜為第一支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二支受遠離損害自他支，不損害自己，也不損害他人，就是不淫欲。好淫欲者傷害自己的精神生命，乃至破壞他人家庭，極不道德。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三支違越所受重修行支，就是不妄語；如果作錯了，要能夠懺悔，這是要不妄語的人才做得到。玄奘大師翻譯的名字實在很忠實，翻譯得這麼長，不直接說不妄語，而說「違越所受重修行支」；意指如果違越所受的戒，不妄語發露懺悔，才能夠重新修行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四支不越所受正念住支，不超越他所受的「正念住」，這要有正念才能夠遠離歌舞倡妓、不坐高廣大床及過午不食，如果不提起正念，沒有辦法做到這三件事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五支不壞正念支，飲酒能夠破壞正念，因此不飲酒這一支是歸納到「不壞正念支」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　論師依於這些理由，將八支歸納成五支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C53-01.htm">近住律儀【八關齋戒】五支八支表</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、顯攝餘2　巳一、攝屬苾芻律儀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二顯攝餘，將比丘律儀、近事律儀、與近住律儀，歸納成在家品及出家品這二類，分二科；第一科攝屬苾芻律儀，說明屬於比丘律儀的範圍內的那些，比丘律儀是指出家戒，還包括了比丘尼戒、正學女（式叉摩那）戒、勤策（沙彌）戒、勤策女（沙彌尼）戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="32092:41106"></a>今於此中，若苾芻尼律儀，若正學、勤策、勤策女律儀，皆在出家品所攝故，當知攝屬苾芻律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這比丘律儀當中，包括比丘尼戒，還有正學女稱為學法女、式叉摩那尼，正學律儀即指式叉摩那尼戒的六法戒。勤策律儀是指沙彌戒，勤策的意思是勤修戒定慧，息滅貪瞋癡。勤策女律儀是沙彌尼戒。所有的出家戒都攝屬在苾芻律儀當中。這一科顯攝餘是說屬於比丘律儀的範圍裡面，包含所有出家戒。換句話說，屬於出家戒的，都歸屬於苾芻律儀。勤策是沙彌，勤策女是沙彌尼。沙彌、沙彌尼要勤於策勵自己成為比丘或比丘尼。沙彌、沙彌尼必須受十戒，十戒其實是將八關齋戒中的離高廣大床、離香花鬘塗、離歌舞倡妓，分成三支，加上離歌舞倡妓及不持金銀寶物，開成沙彌十戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、攝屬近事律儀</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科攝屬近事律儀，說明優婆夷律儀攝屬於近事律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4232"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="11199:41109"></a>若近事女律儀，墮在家品故，相似學所顯故，當知攝屬近事律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果是優婆夷律儀，屬於在家眾受持的五戒，只有少分相似於出家眾的律儀，歸屬於近事律儀，包括優婆塞、優婆夷這二種律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》相似學所顯故者：出家律儀正學處攝，在家律儀少分相似，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　出家的律儀是真正的學處，而在家律儀只是少分的相似於出家戒，只有五條戒，是相似於出家戒的少分，所以才這樣說的。這是屬於近事律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋妨難4　辰一、二眾三眾難2　巳一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋妨難，解釋可能出現的問難，分四科；第一科二眾三眾難，難問出家戒中，為何男眾只有二種律儀，而女眾必須受三種律儀，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何故世尊於苾芻律儀中制立苾芻、勤策二眾律儀，於苾芻尼律儀中制立苾芻尼、正學、勤策女三眾律儀？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼佛在比丘戒當中，只有制立比丘戒、沙彌戒這兩眾的律儀？而在比丘尼戒當中，制立苾芻尼戒，正學女戒、及沙彌尼戒三種律儀呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、答3　午一、標因緣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科標因緣，標示因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由彼母邑多煩惱故，令漸受學苾芻尼律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於女人煩惱很多，根性比較鈍，必須令她漸漸的受學比丘尼律儀。邑，是村，印度人稱女人為母，母可以生很多孩子，像一個村子裡住很多人一樣，母邑即是女人義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋隨應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋隨應，解釋為什麼女眾要制立沙彌尼戒、式叉摩那戒、比丘尼戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於勤策女少分學處深生喜樂，次應授彼正學所有學處。若於正學多分學處深生愛樂，不應率爾授彼具足，必更二年久處習學，若深愛樂，然後當授彼具足戒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　沙彌十戒的內容；第一是不殺生、第二是不偷盜、第三是不淫欲、第四是不妄語、第五不飲酒、第六離高廣大床、第七離香花鬘塗身、第八離歌舞倡妓等、第九離金銀寶物，不捉持金銀寶物、第十離非時食。沙彌十戒與沙彌尼十戒內容一樣，比八關齋戒多一個不持金銀寶物。如果對於沙彌尼戒，少分學出家眾的戒條，能深深歡喜好樂。對於沙彌尼十戒很喜歡好樂，接著應該再教授式叉摩那戒，正式學習比丘尼戒的前方便，傳授六法戒，必須二年內遵守根本戒及六個法：第一不可以染心相觸男子等。第二不能盜人四錢；第三不斷畜生命；第四不妄語；第五不非時食；第六不飲酒；這六種學處是很嚴格的，如有違犯是必須重受式叉摩那戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果女眾喜歡沙彌尼戒，應趕快授她式叉摩那戒；但是，如果她對於式叉摩那戒深深歡喜愛樂，也不可以很快的授她具足戒。必須經過二年之久的學習考驗。若還能夠愛樂學處遵守六法喜歡持戒，這樣才可以授她比丘尼戒。論師主張學人受沙彌尼戒以後，歡喜愛樂持沙彌尼十戒，應該授她式叉摩那尼戒。受完以後，經過二年，再受比丘尼戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、明漸次</span></strong></span></span></p>
