<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：若眼、耳、鼻、舌、身等的相狀不一樣，都不能算是身相。由於這因緣，依眼、耳、鼻、舌、身五根所產生的受，不應該稱為身受？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4258"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：餘有色根不離身故，就彼為名，此復何過。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：因為眼、耳、鼻、舌，這些有色根是不離開身根的，所以就著身的總相來說身受，這樣有什麼過失呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、約意根辨2　申一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科約意根辨，以意根分別，分二科；第一科問，為什麼意識相應受是心受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若不離身故無過者，意根亦爾，不離身轉，依意根受應名身受，是即一切皆是身受，無心受耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果眼耳鼻舌不離開身體，因此依眼耳鼻舌產生的受都應該稱為身受，如果這樣說沒有過失的話，那麼意根也沒有離開身體而活動，所以依著意根接觸法塵產生的受，也應該稱為身受。這樣說起來，一切都是身受，沒有心受了？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、答2　酉一、簡二別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科簡二別，簡別身心二受的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：諸有色根定不離身，意即不爾，故無有過。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：所有的有色根一定都不能離開身體，但是意根是不一樣，不一定與身體在一起活動，依意根接觸法塵產生的受，不稱為身受是沒有過失的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、釋所以</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所以，解釋理由。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？生無色界有情，意根離身而轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這麼說呢？因為無色界的有情，沒有麤的色蘊，意根可以不依色身而單獨活動，所以說依意根觸對法塵所生的受不能稱為身受，而稱為心受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、成所說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科成所說，成立身、心二受的說法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故五根所生諸受合名身受，唯依意者獨名心受。故總說二，謂身、心受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以論主說，眼、耳、鼻、舌、身，接觸色、聲、香、味、觸所生的各種受，合起來可以稱為身受，只有依止意根接觸法塵而產生的受，單獨稱為心受。總說起來有身受及心受的二種受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、共相自性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相自性，說明受的共相自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又一切受皆領納相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所有的受，不論是六種受或是身心二種受都有領納的作用，以領受接納為受的共相。凡夫什麼事來都接受，聖人則不如是，聖人是：「不受一切法得阿羅漢」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大智度論》說，舍利弗的母舅長爪梵志辯才無礙，能辯倒一切外道，可是等到舍利弗的母親懷了舍利弗以後，長爪梵志會辯輸舍利弗的母親，他很生氣，心想：我一定要辯倒她，又外出再求學。很認真的學，連指甲長了都沒時間剪，久而久之指甲變得很長，人們稱他長爪梵志。學成之後回到故鄉向舍利弗挑戰，舍利弗這時已經出家，他再去找佛陀辯論，他說：我不受一切法。佛陀回答他：你這句話接受不接受？長爪梵志心想：如果說受，等於打倒自己。如果說不受，不接受自己這句話肯定輸了。他怎麼說都錯，即默然不語自知輸了，佛因此度他出家修行。當辯論時，舍利弗尊者在旁邊，聽到這句話即證得阿羅漢果。所以說：不受一切法得阿羅漢。凡夫好的也受，壞的也受。他人罵自己，自己全部接受，讚歎自己能全部都接受。其實自己也可以不受。佛說：如果有人罵你，你不接受，罵者會像仰天自唾，還污其面，他罵你的話，全部回歸他自己的身上，你不要接受就沒事了。不過凡夫習慣接受，什麼境界來都接受，使得煩惱很多。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4259"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、想2　卯一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科想，說明想的自性，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等是想自性？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼是想的自性呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、答2　辰一、自相自性2　巳一、標列2　午一、六種2　未一、初六種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科自相自性，說明想蘊的自相自性，又分二科；第一科標列，標列出來，又分二科；第一科六種，有初六種及後六種，分為二種想，又分二科；第一科初六種，說明初六種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：此亦六種，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：想蘊也有六種，是六觸所生想。眼、耳、鼻、舌、身意接觸色、聲、香、味、觸、法時，產生受，因受而有想。六觸所生想，如前面所說的六受一樣，六根接觸六境時，心裡也會想，同時有想心所取相。六觸所生想是初六種想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、後六種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後六種，第二類六種想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又想有六。一、有相想，二、無相想，三、狹小想，四、廣大想，五、無量想，六、無所有想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想又可分成六種；有相想、無相想、狹小想、廣大想、無量想、無所有想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科二種，說明想又可分二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又略有二。一、世間想，二、出世間想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又略有二種想：世間想及出世間想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　世間想是世間人的想法，從欲界乃至非想非非想處天有情的想，仍然執著名言有真實相，這是世間想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　出世間想是指聖人無漏聖慧相應出離三界的想，聲聞行者與人無我想相應，大乘聖人與我法二空真如相應，這都是出世間想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、隨釋6　午一、狹小想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分六科；第一科狹小想，欲纏想名狹小想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">狹小想者，謂欲纏想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為狹小想？纏，是煩惱數數現行。欲界的有情有欲的煩惱想，是狹小想。欲界有情想的範圍不外色、聲、香、味、觸這五種，想來想去不會超過這幾種範圍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、廣大想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣大想，指色纏想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">廣大想者，謂色纏想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　廣大想指取著色界四禪入色界定者的想，及色界眾生的想。色界眾生還在三界裡面，雖然身心光明，還是有色法，並沒有超越解脫色法，且愛味禪定，屬於廣大想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4260"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、無量想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無量想，指空無邊處定及識無邊處定的想，包括入此二種定及生於此二天處眾生的想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無量想者，謂空、識無邊處纏想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無量想指空無邊處與識無邊處有情的想，及入此二種定者的想。纏表示行者還沒有解脫生死，所以是世間想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、無所有想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無所有想，取著無所有的想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無所有想者，謂無所有處纏想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無所有想指執著無所有處定者的想，包括入無所有處定者及生無所有處天眾的想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、有相想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科有相想，說明有相想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此一切名有相想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從欲界一直到無所有處的想，識無邊處想以下的「有所有想」及無所有處的「無所有想」，都是有相想。這些想都沒有超越世間，還是世間的想，還是有三界煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午六、無相想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科無相想，指有頂想及一切出世間學無學想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無相想者，謂有頂想及一切出世間學無學想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相想指非想非非想處想，及一切出世間有學及無學聖者無漏慧相應的想。「有頂」是三有之頂的非想非非想處。入非想非非想處定者及生在非想非非想處的有情，沒有「有想」及「無想」的想，任何想都沒有，乃至無所有處想也沒有。可是也不能說這類有情完全沒有想，因為那一念微微心還存在，是非非想。有頂想的人或入此定者，是屬於無相想，不過仍是凡夫，還是屬於世間想的境界。出世間有學聖者初果到三果的聖人，乃至無學的阿羅漢，他們的想屬於無相想，聖人通達一切法無相，他們有無相想，這是出世間無漏慧相應的想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　根據《顯揚聖教論》卷5說到作意差別有二種。一、有相想、二、無相想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有相想，指除欲界中未善言說者想，第一有想及出世間想，餘有相作意相應想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無相想，指前所除無相作意相應想。」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷1說：「有相想，是指除不善言說，無相界定及有頂定想所餘想。又不善言說想者，謂未學語言故，雖於色起想而不能了此名為色故，名無相想。無相界定想者，謂離色等一切相無相涅槃想故，名無相想。有頂定想者，謂彼想不明利，不能於境圖種種相故，名無相想。」二論對於無相想的解釋文別義同，其中無相想指欲界中未善言說者想，第一有想及出世間無漏想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜集論述記》卷3解釋這段文說：頂是極義，三有之極故名有頂，即非想非非想處想，彼想不明了，不能圖畫（分別）種種境相，雖然於散心時也是無相想。現在從定說要具足明了、分別功能二種才能稱為有相；無相界定（出世間無漏定）雖有明了而不分別，非想非非想處定雖有分別而不明了，嬰孩俱無（沒有定，也沒有明了、分別二種功能），都名為無相，與此相反名有相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　非想非非想處定︰又名非有想非無想定，指超無所有處，更思惟「非想非非想之相」而安住之。此「非想非非想定」無明勝之想，是異於滅盡定，又非無想，故不同於無想定。關於修何等加行始可入非想非非想處定，《法蘊足論》卷8〈無色品〉解釋說︰初修業者，思惟無所有處為苦麤障，謂非想非非想處為靜妙離，修習非想非非想之加行，入非想非非想定。又依《俱舍論》卷28說，前三空定乃約其加行而立名，因其次第修加行時，思惟無邊之空、無邊之識及無所有，因此安立空、識、無所有等名。而第四定，乃約「想」之當體而立名。因為此定無明勝之想，得非想名；有昧劣想，故名非非想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《清淨道論》卷10說無色品，以塗鉢的油來譬喻非想非非想處定想的特性：據說一位沙彌用油塗了鉢而放在那裡，到了飲粥的時候，長老對那沙彌說：「拿鉢來！」他說：「鉢內有油，尊師。」「那麼，沙彌，拿油來，將它倒在油筒裡面去。」沙彌說：「可是沒有油，尊師。」在這個譬喻，因為鉢中塗著油不適用於盛粥之義故說「有油」，然而又沒有油可以倒入油筒故說「無油」，如是而此（非想非非想處之）想不能有利想的作用故「非想」，因有殘餘諸行的細妙狀態的存在故「非非想」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上詳細解釋六種想。從中可以看出所有的學、無學聖者的想，都是出世間想，因為這些聖人都已證得無分別智，通達我空無相的境界。有頂想以下，三界有情的想都是世間想。但是三界有情的想又分二種，有相的想及無相的想；有相想是從欲界一直到無所有處的想，都屬有相想。無相想是非想非非想處想，還沒有超出三界，所以還是世間想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、共相自性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相自性，說明想的共相自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又一切想皆等了相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所有的想都是平等的了相，想的作用是取相，能於所知法，平等取相是所有想的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂有頂想等者：非想非非想處，無如下地麤相想故，名無相想。學無學道證出世間勝義境故，名無相想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼非想非非想處是無相想呢？非想非非想處，沒有無所有處以下的色界或者是欲界等，那些麤相的想，非想非非想處的想很微細若有若無，所以稱為無相想。初果到四果的聖人，證得出世間第一義諦的空相時，屬於無相想，聖人的無相想是出世間想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4261"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、行2　卯一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科行，說明行蘊的自性，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等是行自性？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：行的自性是什麼呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、答2　辰一、自相自性3　巳一、六種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，分二科；第一科自相自性，行蘊的自相自性分為六種、五種、三種的不同，又分三科；第一科六種，說六種分類的自相自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：此亦六種，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　回答：行蘊也有六種，如同前面受蘊所說的一樣，有六觸所生行。由眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意，接觸色、聲、香、味、觸、法時，所生出的六種行的自性。《阿含經》也是這樣說，由六觸可以生出六受、六想、六行、六識，比照前面的六觸所生受，應該了知六種行自性即六觸所生行。這是六種行蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、五種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科五種，行蘊又可以歸納成五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="72115:41472"></a><a name="56899:41472"></a><a name="5644:41472"></a>又此行相，由五種類令心造作。一、為境隨與，二、為彼合會，三、為彼別離，四、能發雜染業，五、令心自在轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又行的相狀，這一念心造作時有五種形態：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、為境隨與：根塵識三和合故，令思心所生起造作，對於所緣境隨順參與領取納受、於可意境思欲和合，於不可意境思欲別離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、為彼合會：這念心希望與境界和合在一起；比如說這是歡喜的境界，內心希望這個境界永遠不要消失，心想要和這個境界合在一起，思心所想要去作某些事情，讓自己與歡喜的境界合在一起，不要分離，通常容易引起貪心的造作，這是我們一般人的心情。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、為彼別離：內心的造作是希望與境界分離；當然這是指不歡喜的境界，如果碰到逆境，大家都希望趕快離開，心就開始造作，想要遠離這種境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、能發雜染業：心裡想要有所造作時，藉由身體、語言、及內心的思惟表現出來。面對境界時，想要和境界在一起，或者和境界別離，會造作雜染的身語意三業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、令心自在轉：通常是指修世間道或世間道成就者，心不受煩惱繫縛，能隨內心的意願，而入世間定或者出世間定。一般沒有修行的人，心受煩惱控制而不自在。然而修禪定或修聖道成功的人，能令心隨智慧行而轉，這是心自在轉。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行蘊的範圍很廣，除受想以外的心所都屬於行蘊，但也可以專指五遍行中的思，此處特以五遍行心所中的思而言。思是內心的造作，用現代話說是「意志」，具有決定的力量，當六根接觸六境時，五遍行心所同時和合運作，思的力量推動這一念心領納境界，這時是「為境隨與」；若是順境，思心所與貪等心所和合推動這念心與境合會；若遇逆境，思心所與瞋等心所和合推動這念心遠離此境。在順逆境中行與貪瞋癡等心所和合，藉由身語意三業的造作，為了達成目的，而發出雜染的業，凡夫的思多半不離貪瞋癡的控制；有一類歡喜修禪定或聖道者，依止禪定或聖道的力量，降伏或斷除貪瞋癡，令心隨智慧的造作（行）而轉，即是「令心自在轉」，這些心裡染淨的活動都是「行」的功能。論主將行的造作歸納成五種，使讀者對行有更詳細的認知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、三種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科三種，說明三種行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此行相略有三種。一者、善行，二、不善行，三、無記行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又心裡的造作，要略而言有善行、不善行、與無記行三種。善行是行與善心所相應；行與不善心所相應，是不善行。行與非善非不善心所相應，是無記行；沒有特別的用意，只是作這件事，如搔頭、抓鼻子，或摸摸臉等，這些屬於無記行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、共相自性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相自性，說明行的共相自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又一切行皆造作相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又一切行共同的相貌是造作相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》為境隨與者：想領納境，此造作思隨與彼力，故下說於所緣境隨與領納。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/55.htm#41477:43021">陵本五十五卷三頁4397</a>）此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想領納境界時，此造作思即隨順推動心去領納境界，於可意境思欲和合，於不可意境思欲別離。所以下文說，於所緣境隨與領納，這裡應準照〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷55，1809頁那段文來理解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅五、識2　卯一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科識，說明識的自性，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4262"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何等是識自性？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：什麼是識的自性呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、答2　辰一、標列2　巳一、六種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標列，標出列舉識蘊，又分二科；第一科六種，識蘊的自性有六種、三種的不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：略有六種。所謂眼識乃至意識，是識自性差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：要略而言有六種識；是眼識、耳識、鼻識、舌識、身識、意識，這是六種識的自性差別，它們各各不同，各有各的特色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、三種2　午一、略</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科三種，分二科；第一科略，要略說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又識有三種。一、領受差別，二、採境差別，三、分位差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又識可分成三種。一、領受差別；二、採境差別；三、分位差別。識有這三種差別的特性。接下來解釋這三種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、廣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣，詳細說明三種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">領受差別有三，採境差別有六，分位差別有三。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　識與受在一起活動時，能領納苦受、樂受、不苦不樂受這三種受，這是領受差別。眼識乃至意識能了別色、聲、香、味、觸、法六境，這是採境差別的六種。分位差別是指識還能了別過去、現在、未來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、總結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總結，總相結說識蘊有十八種自性差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是識蘊差別，總有十八自性應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總結：眼識、耳識、鼻識、舌識、身識、意識六種識，能了別色、聲、香、味、觸、法六境的採境差別，又能領納苦受、樂受、不苦不樂受這三種受，以及過去、現在、未來的三種分位差別，加上眼等六種所依差別，合起來識蘊有十八種自性。識的共相自性是了別，容易明白，也就略而不說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說名諸蘊自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名諸蘊自性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總結以上是色、受、想、行、識五蘊的自性。總辨蘊善巧的第一個部分，分別五蘊中一一蘊的自性。將五蘊的自性複習一下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊：自相自性有可分為十一種，或是二種；十一種是眼、耳、鼻、舌、身，色、聲、香、味、觸以及法處所攝色。二種色蘊是四大種及所造色二種。色蘊的共相體性是變礙性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受蘊：自相自性分成六觸所生受的六種，以及心受及身受二種。受蘊的共相體性是領納相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想蘊：自相自性初六種的六觸所生想，及後六種的有相想、無相想、狹小想、廣大想、無量想、無所有想。又可分為世間想及出世間想二種。想的作用是取相，能於認知法，平等取相是所有想的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行蘊：自相自性分為六種的六觸所生行（思），分為五種是：為境隨與、為彼合會、為彼別離、能發雜染業、令心自在轉。心裡的造作，又有善行、不善行、與無記行三種。行蘊以造作為共相體性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　識蘊：識蘊的自相自性有眼識、耳識、鼻識、舌識、身識、意識的六種識；識又分成三種：領受差別、採境差別、分位差別；若詳細再分，領受苦、樂、捨受三種，採六境的差別，加上過去、現在、未來的分位差別，加上所依差別的六根，總共有十八種。識蘊的共相體性是了別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4263"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》領受差別等者：領納苦樂等受，是名領受差別。取色等境以為所緣，是名採境差別。過去、未來、現在，是名分位差別。如是三種合共十二，并前眼等六種所依，如是識蘊總有十八自性差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　識的領受差別，指識與受和合領納苦受、樂受及不苦不樂受。識能了別色、聲、香、味、觸、法六境，以此為所緣境，這是識的採境差別。過去、現在、未來，識都可以了別境界，稱為分位差別。這三種識的差別自性加起來共有十二種，加上依六根而生六種識，識蘊合起來有十八種自性差別應知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C53-02.htm">識蘊十八自性差別表</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、義2　丑一、雙徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科義，總辨蘊善巧的第二個部分是義，分二科；第一科雙徵，提出二個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，蘊義云何？為顯何義，建立諸蘊？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又蘊的意義是什麼？為了顯示什麼道理，佛陀要建立五蘊呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、別答2　寅一、答蘊義2　卯一、差別義2　辰一、舉色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別答，各別回答，分二科；第一科答蘊義，回答蘊的意義，又分二科；第一科差別義，說明色蘊的差別義，又分二科；第一科舉色，列舉十一種色說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂所有色，若去來今乃至遠近。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所有的色包括自身中由地水火風所組成的色蘊，加上若過去、若未來、若現在、若內、若外、若麤、若細、若劣、若勝、若遠、若近、有十一種色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、例餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘，如色餘蘊也一樣有十一種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如色，乃至識亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如色蘊有十一種，受蘊乃至識蘊也是這樣的觀察，一樣各有十一種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、總略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總略義，總略攝一切蘊，積聚義是蘊義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是總略攝一切蘊，積聚義是蘊義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是將過去、未來、現在、內、外、麤、細、劣、勝、遠、近的五蘊全部要略的歸納成一切蘊。蘊的意思是積聚義，因此說五蘊包涵身心一切的狀況。色、受、想、行、識是一大堆、一大堆積聚在一起，即是蘊的意思。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於五蘊中什麼是內乃至遠近？據《俱舍論頌疏論本》卷1說：「諸所有色若內外等十一種差別，義理上有五門：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、三世門：無常已滅名過去，若未已生名未來，已生未謝名現在。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、內外門：自身名內，所餘他身及非情名外；或約十二處辨眼等五根名內，色等五境名外。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、麤細門：色有三種，一有見有對，指色等五境；二無見有對，指眼等五根，聲香味觸；三無見無對，指無表色。這三色中，有對名麤，無對名細；或相觀待而安立，如無見有對色對望有見有對色，名細；對望無見無對色，名麤。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、劣勝門：染污名劣，不染污名勝。十一種色中，眼等五根及香味觸八種是無記性，色聲二種通三性，無表色唯善惡。於三性中，善無記名不染污，惡名染污。五蘊色心二法若是染污，名劣，若是不染污之善無記名勝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、遠近門，過去未來名遠，現在名近。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如色蘊中有此五門，乃至識蘊也有五門，應知道理也是一樣，唯麤細一門與色蘊有差別，即眼等五識相應之受想行識四蘊，依五根故名麤；第六意識相應受想行識四蘊，唯依意根故名細；或約地辨，指三界九地中，相對而言下地名麤，上地名細。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本論〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1842頁說：已受用因果義，一切是過去；未受用因果義，一切是未來；答已受用因義及未受用果義，一切是現在。內，是指眼等內六處、法處所攝色及依內六處所生的受、想、行、識等心心所法；外，是指外五塵。麤，是指不光潔、積聚、相增長義；細，是麤相違義。相對而言欲界色是麤，色界色是細；欲界的受想行識是麤，色界的受想行識是細；色界的受想行識若觀待於無色界則是麤，無色界的受想行識是三界中最細。劣，指無常、苦、不淨、染污義；妙，是劣相違義。總相而言，三界五蘊相對於出世勝義都是無常、苦、不淨、染污；依世俗諦相對而言，三界九地中欲界五趣雜居地是劣，色界離生喜樂地是勝，依理往上類推，無色界無所有處地是劣，非想非非想處地是勝。遠，是指空間上的處所距離很遠，這唯依色蘊而言，及時間上過去未來，這是通色無色蘊。近，是遠相違義。要略而言，過去未來的五蘊是遠，現在的五蘊是近。其實有情的生命體是一堆一堆的色、受、想、行、識在那裡不斷地現行活動。生命體的現象包括身與心這二部分，用色、受、想、行、識五蘊表示。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若去來今乃至遠近者：謂若過去、若未來、若現在、若內、若外、若麤、若細、若劣、若勝、若遠、若近，如是一切建立色蘊乃至識蘊，是名蘊義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以時間來說，有過去的、未來的、或是現在的色受想行識。以自他的五蘊而說，內是指自身的五蘊，若外是指他人的五蘊。或是外面的色、聲、香、味、觸、法。以有無障礙而說麤細：麤的五蘊，是有障礙的，有對的色法；或細的五蘊，細的是微細的色聲香味觸法。麤的受是苦受及樂受，細的受是不苦不樂受。想行識依理類推，對於五蘊有不同的解釋。以有無染污或以界地而說劣、勝；劣是屬於染污，品質低一點的欲界五蘊。勝指上二界的人，色界、無色界的人品質高一點。「若遠若近」，過去及未來的色、受、想、行、識是離有情比較遠的，現在色、受、想、行、識是離有情比較近。用這幾個方法來分別，建立色蘊乃至識蘊，蘊的意思指積聚。每一種蘊又都有很多的特色，這些的特色積聚起來，是諸多因緣的和合相，是有情的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答建立，回答佛陀為什麼要建立色、受、想、行、識的五蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4264"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由諸蘊唯有種種名性諸行，當知為顯無我性義，建立諸蘊。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於色、受、想、行、識五蘊，只是聖教依八識的心、心所變現之種種法相，而以名言安立假說之法，是眾緣所生、唯識為性的有為諸行而已；世間眾生依第六意識於此諸識生時變似色等蘊相（似我法之相分）執為實我實法。佛憐憫眾生迷惑顛倒，因此為令眾生通達五蘊無我的法性，隨緣施設建立五蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修行者如實通達五蘊無我，可以解脫三界生死輪迴。色蘊不是一直不變，從少到老，不斷在變化當中，不能自在；希望身體不要生病，卻不能不生病。生病了去治病，不見得完全會好。假設醫好了，還會繼續生病，根本是不能自在的。色蘊是依因緣的法則在那裡運作，不是自己能作主的。受也很難控制，所有的境界出現都得接受，苦受時生瞋，樂受生貪，不苦不樂受生癡，真是不自在。如果不如實知想所取相無實，引發雜染，作錯事惹來一身麻煩。凡夫不知道想是無我，沒有經過修行調練的話，即是這樣。行是造作，如果沒有修學佛法，不知道行是無我，會不斷地造業，起心動念無不是業，無不是罪，所作的事不離生死，不出三界。每個人，從生到老，為了生活，為了溫飽，不知要造作多少業，如蠶作繭自作自受。識是了別，從生到死，只要這生命還在，會不斷在了別各種境界，與受、想、行及貪瞋癡等心所和合造作種種的業。為令眾生通達五蘊無我，因此佛陀建立了五蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》唯有種種名性諸行者：假說所依，是謂名性，此即諸行。當知唯由諸蘊所顯，以此諸蘊總攝一切行故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由於諸蘊，若是凡夫世間假說所依，只是第六意識依名言分別諸法時，內心變似種種蘊相，凡夫執此為實有我法成為遍計所執；聖人通達諸蘊無我無實，為令迷心多之眾生而隨緣施設五蘊。世間假說所依是第六意識的虛妄遍計，聖人如實通達遍計執空，假說所依是依他眾緣所生之八識及諸心所，這類五蘊假名所依稱為名性諸蘊，也就是世間一切有為法。應當了知世間一切有為法可以由諸蘊而顯示，也就是說五蘊可以總攝一切有為法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼佛要建立五蘊呢？佛為了令眾生通達五蘊無我的真實義。其實人是不自在的，不像所想像的在因地時要造作就造作，受果時由不得己，哪裡能自在呢？造業時，怎麼樣造都可以，但是受果報時，沒有一個人受得了。苦果現前時，大家都是唉唉叫，可知五蘊是無我的，不自在的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、差別5　丑一、色蘊2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科差別，總相辨明蘊善巧的第三部分是差別，分五科；第一科色蘊，說明色蘊，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，云何色蘊差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又色蘊有什麼差別相呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標列，標列六種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">略由六種。一、由事故；二、由相故；三、由識執不執故；四、由識空不空故；五、由想所行故；六、由邊際故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略而言，色蘊有六種差別相。一、由事說明色蘊體性；二、由相說明色蘊的自相和共相；三、由識執不執受色的差別，由識有執受或者是沒有執受，說明色蘊差別；四、由識空不空，由識是否與根一起活動，來說明色蘊差別；五、由想所行：色蘊是想心所活動的境界；六、由邊際，說明色的最高邊際，是到色界第四禪天。論主由這六個角度來說明色蘊的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋6　辰一、事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，隨著一一法各別解釋，分六科；第一科事，由事解釋色蘊的特性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">事者，謂所有諸色皆是四大種及四大種所造。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　事的特性，是指所有的色法都是四大種及四大種所造色和合而成。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、相2　巳一、自相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科相，隨釋色蘊的相差別，分二科；第一科自相，解說自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">相者，略有三種。一、清淨色，二、清淨所取色，三、意所取色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略而言色蘊的自相有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、清淨色：眼、耳、鼻、舌、身根五淨色根，都是清淨色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、清淨所取色：色、聲、香、味、觸五塵就是清淨所取色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、意所取色：就是法處所攝色。意識隨著前五識現量了別色塵以後，再進一步分別所取的色，這是眼等五俱意識。或是獨頭意識所緣取的色塵，也是法處所攝色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《顯揚聖教論》卷1，13頁：「法處所攝色，謂一切時意所行境，色蘊所攝，無見無對。此復三種。謂律儀色、不律儀色、及三摩地所行境色。」法處所攝色，指過去、現在、未來一切時意識所緣，屬於色蘊的法塵，它的性質是無見無對，看不到也沒有質礙性。它的範圍包括戒體的律儀色、現行十惡業的不律儀色，及三摩地所行色的下中上三品定中所緣影像色性及定果色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜集論》卷1，8頁：「法處所攝色者：略有五種。謂極略色、極迥色、受所引色、遍計所起色、自在所生色。」法處所攝色的五種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、極略色：指名言假安立的極微色，這是分析色聲香味觸五境，眼耳鼻舌身五根，或地水火風四大種等一切具有質礙性之實色至最小單位時，名極微。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、極迥色：即分析空界色，明、闇等不具質礙性之顯色令至極微。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、受所引色：即無表色，依身口發動了善惡業，而後產生了無形的色法，是一種不能表現於外的色法，如戒體是由受戒所引發的，有防非止惡的作用。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、遍計所起色：意識產生周徧計度虛妄分別的作用，在心內所變現之影像色，如空中花、水中月、鏡中像等皆屬此類，具有影像無所依托之自體。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、自在所生色：指由禪定力所變現之色聲香味觸等境，凡夫之禪定力所變現者為假色不能實用，八地以上聖者大威德定所變為可實用之色法，如變糞土成黃金，可令眾生受用。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大乘唯識學者認為前四色屬假色，第五色通假實。聲聞乘說一切有部等則認為極略色、極迥色乃至受所引色等，皆為具有實體之色法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、共相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相，色蘊以變礙為共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又變礙相是色共相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊無常變化、佔有空間有質礙，所以說變礙相，是色蘊的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4265"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、識執不執2　巳一、執受色3　午一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科識執不執，隨釋色蘊的識執不執受色來分別，分二科；第一科執受色，說明執受色，又分三科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">識執不執者，若識依執，名執受色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有識執受的色法是執受色，沒有識執受的色法，是非執受色。如身體有識執受的部分，受到傷害時會有痛的感覺；如沒有識執受的地方是不會痛覺，如頭髮、指甲，因此剪頭髮不覺得痛，但是髮根是執受色，它有識的執受，拔頭髮時會感覺痛。這是說由有識執受的色法與識不執受的色法的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復云何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這又怎麼說呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、釋2　未一、由識託</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科由識託，識託付在色法上面，識與色法同安危。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂識所託，安危事同，和合生長。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為識託付在色法上面，識與色法同安危，如果此色法受到損害，識也不能存在。如果身體壞了，識也沒有辦法存在，就得離開。從入胎開始乃至死亡以前都是這樣，識依住於色身，識與色身和合生長，生命才能相續，所以色心不能相離。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、由生受</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由生受，執受色因為有識在，所以能生出感受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此為依，能生諸受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又識依止於色身，識活動時，就能夠生出感受。識和色是不能分離的。有識執受色法及沒有執受的色法，有這樣差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、非執受色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科非執受色，說明非執受色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">與此相違，非執受色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　沒有識執受的色法，如山河大地、花草樹木等，不會有感受。像敲打椅子，它不會有感受，也不會向你抱怨。有執受色的內身與沒有執受色的外五塵作用不一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、識空不空2　巳一、同分色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科識空不空，隨釋色蘊空不空，以識是否與根一起活動來分別色蘊的差別，分二科；第一科同分色，說明同分色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">識空不空者，若識不空，名同分色，由此與識等義轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　識空與不空是什麼意思呢？如果色根取境時，識不空即稱為同分色。等，是平等、相等。義，是指境界，由於根與識在同一個境界上活動，稱為同分色。譬如現在眼睛正在看一朵蘭花，這時眼識與眼根同時在蘭花上面活動，那麼眼根即是同分色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4266"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、彼同分色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科彼同分色，識不依色根了境，色根相似相續活動。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若識空者，名彼同分色，似自相續而隨轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若識不與根一起活動時，色根本身仍然相似相續的存在，這時的色根稱為彼同分色。舉眼根為例，若眼識不與眼根一起活動時，眼根還是相似相續的存在，這是視而不見的情況，這時的眼根即是彼同分色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》識空不空等者：集論中說：謂不離識，彼相似根於境相續生故；離識自相，似相續生故，是同分彼同分義。（集論三卷四頁）雜集論釋云：初是同分，諸根與識俱識相似，於諸境界相續生故，由根與識相似轉義，說名同分。第二是彼同分，諸根離識自類相似相續生故，由根不與識合，唯自體相似相續生，根根相相似義，說名彼同分。（雜集論五卷七頁）由是當知名同分色。彼同分色，謂彼色根於色根中，識有空不空義，由或現行不現行故。若識現行，名識不空。識不現行，說名識空。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無著菩薩造的《集論》中解釋同分與彼同分；同分是指不離識，指色根與識和合運轉，識不離根，同時相續取境而轉。彼同分是指離識，識不與根和合運轉，根自相似相續而生，稱為彼同分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜集論》是安慧菩薩根據無著菩薩七卷《集論》，解釋演繹成十一卷，名《雜集論》。《雜集論》先解釋同分。同分指根與識和合運轉，在諸多所緣境上相續活動，由於根與識緣取相同的所緣境，識也了別這個境相，稱為同分。彼同分是說諸根不與識和合運轉，可是諸根還是相似相續的活動，並沒有斷滅，但是根不與識和合運轉，根自體相似相續生稱為彼同分。如眼根繼續在看，可是眼識已經緣到別地方去，這時是視而不見，但根還在，稱為彼同分，不過已經心不在焉，視而不見，聽而不聞，這時是彼同分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之同分色是指識與根同緣一境和合運轉，彼同分色指識不發生作用的根。如有一人去偷黃金，只看到黃金，沒有看到旁邊有人。當他被抓以後，國王問他：「你為什麼在那麼多人面前還敢偷黃金？」他說：「我只有看到黃金，其他人我都沒看到」。相對於黃金比喻是同分色。相對於他所看不到的人，是彼同分色。由此可知同分色及彼同分色的差別。有識與色根和合運轉時，有時識不發生作用，因此有識空不空的差別；識空不空是由識有沒有現行來判別，如果識現行與根一起活動，是識不空，也是同分色。識不現行時，是識空，也是彼同分色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、想所行2　巳一、出種類2　午一、能緣色想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科想所行，隨釋色蘊的想所活動的地方，分二科；第一科出種類，說明想活動的種類，又分二科；第一科能緣色想，說明各種能緣色想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">想所行者，謂緣色想，略有三種。一者、色想，二、有對想，三、別異想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想有取相的功能，能緣的色想略有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、色想：想心所能緣取色境；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有對想：想心所能緣取有質礙的色境。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、別異想：想心所能夠緣取男、女、高、矮、胖、瘦，各種不同的色相，都是想的分別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想心所緣取色境有這三種差別想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、所緣色相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科所緣色相，所緣的色相也有三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">色相亦三，一、有光影相，二、據方處相，三、積集住相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能緣的是色想，所緣的是色相，能緣的想是心；所緣的是相，色的相貌。想所緣的色相也有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有光影相，是青黃赤白，光影明闇、雲煙塵霧等，這些顯色的有光影相，有光明、有影子的色相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、據方處相，想所緣有體相的色法佔有空間；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、積集住相，想緣的色法由諸多地水火風積聚在一起而形成長短、方圓、男女、大小、屋宅、田舍等形狀的色相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋所行3　午一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所行，解釋想在色相上的活動的情況，分三科；第一科略標，要略標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是三相，隨其次第三想所行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說的光影相、據方處所、及積集住相，這三種色相隨著次第，對應三種能緣的色想：色想、有對想、別異想；色想能取有光影相，有對想取據方處相，別異想取積集住相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、別釋3　未一、色想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別解釋，分三科；第一科色想，取青等相，名為色想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4267"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="74084:41544"></a><a name="69400:41544"></a>取青等相，名為色想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能緣取青黃赤白、光影明闇、雲煙塵霧等這些顯色的想，名為色想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、有對想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有對想，能緣取有質礙性的色法，名有對想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能取行礙，名有對想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想心所能緣取有體積、佔有空間、具障礙性的色法，名是有對想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、別異想</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科別異想，能緣取男、女等差別相，名別異想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能取男、女、舍、田等假，名別異想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想心所能緣取的男、女、舍、田等，地水火風和合積聚而成的假相，並無實體性的色，只是假名安立而不是依他緣生的實色。想心所能緣慮諸多色聚和合的不同假相，名別異想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、總結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科總結，總結想所行差別名。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名想所行差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總結以上所說色想能取青黃等有光影相，有對想能緣取具有體積佔有空間的山河大地的實色，別異想能取男女等差別色想，這些都是想心所，緣慮色蘊的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰六、邊際2　巳一、出種別2　午一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科邊際，解釋色蘊差別的界限，分二科；第一科出種別，說出色蘊邊際的種類差別，又分二科；第一科略標，要略標示出色邊際有二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邊際者，謂色邊際略有二種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　邊際是指界限或範圍。色蘊的邊際界限略有二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、列釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列釋，列出來解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4268"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、墮下界，謂欲纏色；二、墮中界，謂色纏色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色蘊有二種界限：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、墮於下界，是有欲界煩惱繫縛的根身器界的色法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、墮於中界，是有色界煩惱繫縛的根身器界的色法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上界的無色界沒有色，所以沒有列出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、簡所說2　午一、標非</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科簡所說，簡別上面沒有說到的無色界色，無色界沒有業報所感得的色法，但有定自在所生的色法，分二科；第一科標非，標出無色界沒有業果色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知此中，就業增上所生諸色，說無色界無有諸色，非就勝定自在色說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前所說色邊際有欲界色、及色界色，是以業力增上所感得的果報而言。無色界天的有情由業力所感得的果報是沒有色法的，此處不是以勝定自在色說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無色界天的有情由於有甚深的禪定，定力很強，解脫自在，能心想事成，隨欲成就色法。無色界的有情，由於定力很強，也可以緣欲界及色界的色法，如果想要色法現前，即可以現前。通常無色界的有情有高慢心，生到上地，沒有色法繫縛，是大安樂境界，對於下地的欲界及色界的境界，覺得粗鄙下劣，很少緣下二界的色法。大正藏的《增壹阿含經》說，色界天及無色界天的天人，知道舍利弗要入涅槃了，他們流的淚像下微細的雨一樣，無色界天人流的淚，像細細的毛毛雨，由此可見無色界天眾也有勝定自在色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、釋由</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋由，解釋理由。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？由彼勝定於一切色皆得自在，諸定加行令現前故，當知此色名極微細定所生色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為何說無色界天眾也有色法？因為他們有殊勝的禪定，對於一切的色法都能夠勝解自在。依止禪定的加行，只要入定即可以使色法現前。無色界並不是沒有色，若想要有身體，只要入定一想即可以變現出一個身體來。無色界天眾的色法是非常微細的定所勝解出來的色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上說到色蘊的邊際有二種，包括欲纏色及色纏色，又將無色界天的色也解釋明白。無色界天其實也有色，不過其中的色是極微細的禪定所生的色。以上是色蘊的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下面要說受蘊的差別，主要內容是從五方面來觀察受蘊的差別：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由事來觀察受的體性，受事是指能領納的受心所，以及隨順生受的根境觸等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、受蘊的相，包括自相及共相。自相有三種：樂受、苦受、不苦不樂受。受的共相是苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、受的生起，以十六觸（有對觸、增語觸、明觸、無明觸、非明非無明觸、愛觸、恚觸、順樂受觸、順苦受觸、順不苦不樂受觸、眼觸、耳觸、鼻觸、舌觸、身觸、意觸）為因緣而生受，分四：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1. 六觸生受，由眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意接觸色、聲、香、味、觸、法引生的受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2. 增語觸，是第六意識依名言來認識一切境界。名為先故想，想為先故說。以如幻如化的因緣生法而言，語言是增加上去的，由增語觸也能生受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3. 順樂受觸、順苦受觸、及順不苦不樂受觸，引生不同的受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4. 由內心的雜染或清淨而有愛、恚、明、無明、非明非無明觸，由這些觸產生不同的受。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、如何觀察受蘊？包括觀察受自性，現法受的生滅因緣，未來受的生滅因緣，受的愛味、過患及出離等，從受的觀察中修毗鉢舍那建立聖道，這是修行方法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由出離，用八個方法來觀察，歸納是苦、集、滅、道四諦。不斷觀修最後能出離苦受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、受蘊2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科受蘊，說明受蘊的差別相，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，云何受蘊差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又什麼是受蘊的差別相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">略由五種。一、由事故；二、由相故；三、由生故；四、由觀察故；五、由出離故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受蘊要略言有五種差別相：由事故、由相故、由生故、由觀察故、由出離故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋5　辰一、事</span></strong></span></span></p>
