<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著一一解釋，分五科；第一科事，由事說明受的特性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">事者，謂領納及順領納法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　事指因緣所生法，亦即受蘊的特性，包括領納的受心所，及隨順生受的因緣：根、境、觸及其它心所法等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4269"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、相2　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科相，解釋受蘊的差別相，分二科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">相者，謂自相及共相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受蘊相包括受蘊的自相及共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、辨2　午一、自相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨，分別受蘊自相、共相的特性，分二科；第一科自相，說明自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自相有三。樂受、苦受、不苦不樂受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受蘊的自相有三種：樂受、苦受、不苦不樂受。這三受通於前六轉識，第六意識另有憂喜二受，共有五受相應，第七識及第八識唯不苦不樂受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、共相2　未一、顯義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相，說明共相，分二科；第一科顯義，顯示苦是受蘊的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">樂受，壞苦故苦；苦受，苦苦故苦；不苦不樂受，行苦故苦。由此因緣，諸所有受皆說名苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樂受現前時快樂，變壞時令人痛苦，這是壞苦；苦受自相即苦，這是苦苦；不苦不樂受由於諸行遷流不息，勢必遭逢壞苦、苦苦；由行苦故苦，這是行苦。由這些因緣觀察諸受，樂受壞苦，苦受苦苦，不苦不樂受行苦，不論是樂受、苦受、或不苦不樂受，共同的相貌都是苦，所以苦是受蘊的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、結名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結名，結名受共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名受共相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是故諸受皆苦，所以苦是受蘊的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、生5　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科生，解釋受蘊生起的因緣差別，分五科；第一科標，標出十六觸為生受的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">生者，謂一切受十六觸所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生者指生受的因緣，一切受都因十六觸而引生的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等十六？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪十六種觸能生受呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4270"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出十六種觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="71327:41582"></a>謂眼觸、耳觸、鼻觸、舌觸、身觸、意觸、有對觸、增語觸、順樂受觸、順苦受觸、順不苦不樂受觸、愛觸、恚觸、明觸、無明觸、非明非無明觸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受生起的因緣共有十六種：眼觸、耳觸、鼻觸、舌觸、身觸、意觸、有對觸、增語觸、順樂受觸、順苦受觸、順不苦不樂受觸、愛觸、恚觸、明觸、無明觸、非明非無明觸。由所依的六根不同，而建立六觸。六觸是指眼觸、耳觸、鼻觸、舌觸、身觸及意觸。有對觸指五識身相應的觸。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大毘婆娑論》卷149：說前五識所緣的色聲香味觸是有對法，有質礙性，所以稱為有對觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、釋4　午一、六觸及有能觸</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科六觸及有能觸，說明六觸及有能觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由所依及所取境故，建立六觸及有對觸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由六種所依根，而建立眼等六觸；由五識緣取的境界都屬有對法，建立有對觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由所依及所取境故等者：謂由所依，建立眼觸乃至意觸；由所取境，建立有對觸應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由所依六根，而建立眼觸、耳觸、鼻觸、舌觸、身觸、乃至意觸。所取境是指五識所緣的境界，色、聲、香、味、觸，都屬有對色法，前五識缘五色麈名為有對觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、增語觸</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科增語觸，意識相應的意觸，又名增語觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由分別境故，建立增語觸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　增語觸是由於意識以名言分別境界，而建立增語觸。第六意識了別境界時，不像前五識可以緣取色、聲、香、味、觸的本質境，第六意識是用名言來認識所緣境，而生起意觸。名言是指語言，因緣生法本身沒有名言，名言是增加上去的，因此稱為「增語觸」。前面讀過，名為先故想，想為先故說，要有名言才能以想去取相，想了之後才能說出話。第六意識以名言為緣，事本無名，名是增語，故建立增語觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由分別境故等者：心所起相，名分別境。言增語者，謂一切眾同類相應名。如攝釋分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/81.htm#41588:61977">陵本八十一卷三頁6170</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　內心所現起的法相，是所分別的境相，這不是由識直接緣取本質境，卻是由內心分別所產生的法塵為分別境。增語觸是指一切諸多同類相應名字，與意識相應，而產生的意觸。如這是茶杯，那是桌子等，各式各樣的東西，及與這些物品相應的名字，都是增語。由於觀待因緣所生的事物，而安立的假名，即是增語。在〈攝釋分〉卷81，2446頁中還會解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、順樂受等觸</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科順樂受等觸，說明順樂受觸、順苦受觸及順不苦不樂受觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由領納境故，建立順樂受等觸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　領納是接受、領受，內心接受境界時，隨順如意可愛的境界而生起樂受，隨順不如意不可愛的境界而生起苦受，隨順非可愛非不可愛境生起不苦不樂受，因此而建立順樂受觸、順苦受觸及順不苦不樂受觸，由觸對境界不同而產生苦、樂、不苦不樂等受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4271"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、愛恚等觸</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科愛恚等觸，說明愛觸、恚觸、明觸、無明觸及非明非無明觸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由染淨故，建立愛、恚、明、無明、非明非無明觸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是以內心的染淨，與煩惱相應或與清淨相應而生起的觸，由此因緣建立愛、恚、明、無明、非明非無明觸。觸對境界的同時有愛煩惱的活動，是愛觸，愛觸所生受，能令人貪執不捨。瞋恚心相應的觸是有瞋心觸境所生起的受，令人厭捨。明觸的明是指聖人有明相應觸，有與智慧相應的無漏觸；接觸一切境界時，心內能通達我空或我法二空真如，了知境界如幻如化無我無我所，一切時安住最上捨，是明觸。明觸所生受不外喜樂捨三受。無明觸是無明相應觸；凡夫不知諸法如幻如化，觸對境界時執實又執我、我所，引生種種煩惱，是無明觸。非明非無明觸是指有漏善觸，有漏善法不是惡法，但也不是聖者的明相應觸，因為還是有漏的，所以是非明。非明是指非明相應觸，非無明是遮止煩惱相應的觸，所以有漏善觸也名非染有漏觸，也是非明非無明觸。凡夫修有漏善的非明非無明觸時，若是歡喜心即生樂受，若是勉強而為，或他人所引也可能也有苦受或捨受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科結，結名受生差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名受生差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由所依六根，建立六觸；前五識領納前五塵所生觸，名有對觸。由意識分別境建立增語觸。由領納境順生苦樂捨受的不同而建立順樂受等三觸。由內心的染淨，而建立愛、恚、明、無明、及非明非無明觸。這十六種觸涵蓋凡聖觸境的不同，是生受的因緣與差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、觀察2　巳一、釋2　午一、明觀察2　未一、起觀2　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科觀察，觀察受蘊的差別，分二科；第一科釋，解釋受蘊差別，又分二科；第一科明觀察，說明如何觀察受蘊，又分二科；第一科起觀，如何可以從苦受當中解脫出來？這一科很重要，又分二科；第一科標，說明如何修無我觀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="73394:41598"></a><a name="49960:41598"></a>觀察差別者，一切如來應正等覺出現世間，皆於諸受起八種觀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觀察諸受的種種差別，諸佛慈悲的在人間示現成佛，開示修行的法門，諸佛對於受都作這八種的觀察。一切如來，指十方三世一切諸佛。應，指諸佛應該受人天的供養，因為諸佛的福慧圓滿。佛是應供，應受人天供養，也是正等覺，佛圓滿地覺悟諸法實相，成就無上正等正覺。正覺是以佛所成就的根本無分別智而說的；等覺則指後得智。這八種對受的觀察，如〈本地分‧菩薩地〉卷44中，菩薩善知世間所說。佛出現世間示現成佛，佛是怎麼樣觀察內心生起的覺受，佛弟子應該向佛學習怎麼樣觀察覺受，才能成就聖道出離三界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出受的八種觀察。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂受有幾種？誰為受集？誰是受滅？誰是受集趣行？誰是受滅趣行？誰是受愛味？誰是受過患？誰是受出離？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　列出對受的八種觀察：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、受有哪幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、生受的因緣是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、令受寂滅的因緣是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、是什麼因緣集聚下一生的受？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、是什麼因緣能令來生的受寂滅不生？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、什麼是受愛味的相貌？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、對於受有愛味，有什麼過患呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、怎麼樣可以斷除出離受的愛味煩惱呢？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是諸佛對受的八種觀察。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、證知</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科證知，佛以八相觀察諸受以後，證明、及體驗到受的實相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是觀時，如實了知受有三種，觸集故受集。應知如經分別廣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛對於受，作這八種觀察之後，如受的實相而了知受有樂受、苦受、和不苦不樂受三種，這是回答第一種觀察，受有幾種？因為有觸就有受，前文說過凡聖共有十六種觸，這些觸都是生受的因緣。關於受的觀察應知在《阿含經》中有詳細分別，請參考《雜阿含經》卷2 所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、顯略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯略義，要略顯示八種觀察諸受的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4272"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是八種觀察諸受，當知略顯自相觀、現法轉因觀、彼滅觀、後法轉因觀、彼滅觀、彼二轉因觀、彼二轉滅因觀，及清淨觀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這八種觀察諸受，要略顯示如下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、自相觀：觀察受有幾種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、現法轉因觀：是「誰為受集？」現法五蘊生起受的因緣，現在的受，是因為觸集故受集。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、彼滅觀：指「誰是受滅？」什麼因緣滅，受才會滅？應該說觸滅受就滅。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、後法轉因觀：是「誰是受集趣行？」觀察什麼因緣生起後法的受。觸對境界產生各種感受以後，隨順諸受生出種種的愛憎心情，緣愛有取，緣取有下一生的苦果。後法轉因觀也可以說是觀惑業；因為有受，而起惑造業，造業後，還會再得到下一個生命體，輪迴的苦果是沒完沒了，一生接一生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、彼滅觀：是「誰是受滅趣行？」有什麼方法可以使後法的受寂滅不生？這是觀道諦；方法很多，如四念處、四正勤、四如意足、五根、五力、七覺支、八正道分等三十七道品都是受滅趣行。《阿含經》說這即是八正道，如果修八正道成功了，可以滅除來生的苦受。再將彼滅觀縮小範圍，是觀受無我、無我所，成功了，可以從受出離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、彼二轉因觀：「二」是指現法及後法。觀察什麼原因，有現在的生命體，又引生出未來的生命體；為什麼會得到現在的果報？這一念心，現在的受即是現在生命體的果報，下一生還會有受，原因在那裡？這是配合「誰是受愛味？」的觀察。對於受生起種種的愛憎煩惱，是使有情現在果報相續與未來果報生起的主要原因。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、彼二轉滅因觀：用什麼方法可以使有情滅除現法及後法受？這是配合「誰是受過患？」觀察受的過患，因而斷除受的愛味，能寂滅現法受及後法受。受的過患是什麼？受的共相是苦，《阿含經》說無常、苦、空、無我，道理是一樣的。因為苦，所以無我、不自在，乃至起惑造業純大苦聚，這些都是受的過患。觀察受的過患是通向滅除受的主因，所以就是「彼二轉滅觀」。「二」是指現在的受和未來的受，就是現在的生命體和未來的生命體這二種。有生命體就有受，受是果報，每一個人從生到死都有種種的感受，領受種種不同的果報，想要消滅果報的生起，必須知道受的過患。如果不知過患，是不能厭離受的愛味，也不能滅去現法受及後法受，因此要觀察受的過患。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、及清淨觀：是觀察「誰是受出離？」受出離有幾種情況？出離受的方法有世間的禪定及出世間的聖道，下文將詳細解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結名觀察差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名觀察差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於受，應該要作這八種觀察，能出離苦，得到解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知略顯自相觀等者：觀受自性，名自相觀。觀彼現在流轉因緣，名現法轉因觀。觀彼現在還滅因緣，名彼滅觀。觀彼當來流轉因緣，名後法轉因觀。觀彼當來還滅因緣，名彼滅觀。觀彼後法、現法雜染因緣，名彼二轉因觀。觀彼後法、現法清淨因緣，名彼二轉滅因觀。觀離雜染，名清淨觀。如是八種觀察行相，如次配釋前說受相八種差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觀受本身不共於它法的體性，名受的自性，這是「自相觀」。受的自性，包括樂受、苦受、不苦不樂受。觀察在現在生命體中的受，不斷地生起、轉變、滅去的因緣，是「現法轉因觀」。觀察受出現在現在的生命體上的原因，是「觀彼現在流轉因緣」，經上說：緣觸有受，觸集故受集。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觀察使令現在生命體的受，寂滅止息的因緣是什麼？這是「彼滅觀」，經上說：觸滅故受滅。觀察受將來還會相續轉變生起的因緣，是「後法轉因觀」。若觀「誰是受集趣行？」由於受的出現而生後有愛，由愛而有取，緣取會有有，緣有會再生起下一個生命體，這是觀彼當來流轉因緣，名「後法轉因觀。」。觀察如何使令未來的生命體，不再生起受，使得受能寂滅止息的因緣，這是「彼滅觀」，是屬於道諦的觀察。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　用什麼方法使令後法受不再生起，要修我空觀、法空觀等無漏聖道，成就之後，才能斷除生死輪迴不生後法受。這也就是「誰是受滅趣行？」，與「誰是受滅？」有一點差別，因為「趣行」的「行」是指有為法的道諦，「趣行」是指寂滅諸受的修行，必須修學聖道才能寂滅諸受，修道的方法是屬於有為法；而「誰是受滅？」，指什麼因緣滅了，受才會滅？應該說觸滅了受就滅，這是屬於滅諦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　觀察由受生起現法及後法雜染的因緣，稱為「觀彼後法、現法雜染因緣」，是觀「誰是受愛味？」如果對受有愛味，因之起惑造業，這是生起現法受及後法受的因緣，是「彼二轉因觀」。觀察出離現法受及後法受，令心清淨的因緣，是「名彼二轉滅因觀」。要出離現法受及後法受要觀察「誰是受過患？」認識受的過患，去除對受的愛味，才能出離現法受，令後法受寂滅不生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一般很少人知道快樂及捨受也有過患，大家都知道痛苦有過患，想趕快出離，可是佛法告訴眾生諸受皆苦，應該要出離所有的受，包括樂受及捨受。《金剛經》說：發阿耨多羅三藐三菩提心的菩薩摩訶薩，應令一切眾生入無餘涅槃而滅度之。最究竟的境界，是要到無餘涅槃去，涅槃是無為法無有諸受。如何達到這程度？是要觀察諸受苦、空、無常、無我，滅除煩惱才能證得涅槃。如果出離受的愛味即能解脫，解脫得清淨，這是「清淨觀」。這八種觀察行相是配合前面所說的「受相八種差別」觀察，是前文說的：受有幾種？誰為受集？誰是受滅？誰是受集趣行？誰是受滅趣行？誰是受愛味？誰是受過患？誰是受出離？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C53-03.htm">於受八種觀察表</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、出離2　巳一、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科出離，說明受蘊的出離，分二科；第一科釋，解釋受的出離差別；依禪定力可出離苦樂憂喜受，依聖道出離捨受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">出離者，謂初靜慮出離憂根，第二靜慮出離苦根，第三靜慮出離喜根，第四靜慮出離樂根，於無相界出離捨根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依禪定及聖道力可以出離苦樂憂喜捨五受。證得初禪，必定遠離欲界的欲恚害三種煩惱，離欲則無憂，初禪可以出離憂根。第二禪出離苦根，二禪眼耳身三識不轉，進一步能出離苦根。第三禪遠離二禪喜受的愛味，能出離喜根。第四禪遠離三禪樂受的愛味，出離樂根。聖者成就無相三昧能超越四禪的捨根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結名出離差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名出離差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是出離諸受的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂初靜慮出離憂根等者：三摩呬多地中別釋其相應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/11.htm#41613:8594">陵本十一卷十頁880</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初禪出離憂根乃至無相界出離捨根的內容，在〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷11中已各別詳細解釋其相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4273"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、想蘊2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科想蘊，由五方面說明想蘊的差別，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，云何想蘊差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又什麼是想蘊的差別相？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出想蘊五種差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">略由五種。一、由事故；二、由相故；三、由顛倒故；四、由無顛倒故；五、由分別故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想蘊的差別相要略而言有五種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由事：想蘊的體性差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由相：想蘊的自相共相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由顛倒：執著常樂我淨的想倒及心倒、見倒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、由無顛倒：了知想蘊無常苦空無我，正取相轉，心、見皆無顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由分別：有五種想分別相：境界分別、領納分別、假設分別、虛妄分別、實義分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋5　辰一、事</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，解釋想蘊的五種差別相，分五科；第一科事，由事說明想蘊的特性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">事者，謂取所緣相及隨順彼法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　事是指想蘊的特性，想蘊能取所緣的境相，以名句文身熏習而生想蘊，取所緣相是想蘊本身的特性，隨順彼法是指成就想蘊的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨順彼法者：名句文身熏習為緣，想乃得生，由是說名隨順彼法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由名句文身熏習為緣而有想蘊，想依名言能取境相，名句文身的熏習，是生起想蘊的主要因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、相2　巳一、釋2　午一、自相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科相，隨釋想的相狀差別，分二科；第一科釋，解釋，又分二科；第一科自相，說明想蘊的自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">相者，自相有六種，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想蘊的相狀有自相及共相二種。前文說想蘊有二種自相，第一種六觸所生想，第二種：有相想、無相想、狹小想、廣大想、無量想、無所有想。這些都屬於想蘊的自相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、共相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科共相，說明想蘊的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4274"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">等了相是共相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　平等了達境相是想蘊的共相。想以取相為用，所取相與所緣事平等，能知事相說名：了。等了相，是一切想的共相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說名相差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名相差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六觸所生想及有相想等六種想，是想蘊的自相，等了相是想蘊的共相，這是想的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、顛倒2　巳一、第一義2　午一、釋2　未一、想倒2　申一、舉於無常計常</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顛倒，解釋想蘊的想顛倒差別，有第一義及第二義，分二科；第一科第一義，約第一義解釋，又分二科；第一科釋，解釋，又分二科；第一科想倒，說明第一義的想顛倒，又分二科；第一科舉於無常計常，於所緣境執取常樂我淨名想倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顛倒差別者，謂諸愚夫無所知曉，隨逐無明起不如理作意，於所緣境無常計常，取相而轉，是名想倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　顛倒差別，是指凡夫不知諸法實相，隨著無明煩惱起不如理作意，於一切所緣境無常執以為常，顛倒取著常相而轉，這是想倒。只要未斷無明，一切時處都有想倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、例於苦計樂等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於苦計樂等，凡夫執苦為樂、不淨為淨、無我為我，也都是想倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如於無常計常，如是於苦計樂、於不淨計淨、於無我計我。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　凡夫由於無常倒執為常，以至苦倒執為樂，不淨倒執為淨，無我倒執為我，這些都是顛倒想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、心倒等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科心倒等，說明心倒及見倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此想顛倒，諸在家者能發心倒，一分出家者能發見倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　凡夫常樂我淨的顛倒想，令諸在家人發起貪瞋癡的心倒，隨逐愛樂五欲；也使令一部分出家人妄執邪見，不如實知生死涅槃實相，產生增上慢而發出錯誤的思想，這是見倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說名顛倒差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名顛倒差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上所說，凡夫有想倒，倒執根身器界等所缘境為常，以至樂我淨，因想倒而生心倒或見倒，這些都是想顛倒的差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4275"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、第二義3　午一、想倒</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，說明第二類顛倒想，分三科；第一科想倒，於身受心法四事邪取常樂我淨相的想倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此想顛倒復有差別。謂於四事邪取其相，是名想倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想顛倒另有差別義，是凡夫於不淨的身體邪執為淨相，諸受皆苦妄取一分為樂，剎那生滅無常變化之心妄取常相，因緣生法不自在、無我妄執為我，在身受心法四種因緣所生法上顛倒取相，是第二類的想倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、心倒</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科心倒，想倒為依於境生貪等煩惱名心倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由如是等了相故，於境貪著，是名心倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若依此常樂我淨顛倒想，於身受心法境上生自體愛及境界愛等煩惱，稱為心倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、見倒</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科見倒，由於顛倒想，妄執邪見為勝的見倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由如是等了相故，有執著者，於顛倒事堅執、忍可、開示、建立，是名見倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若於境界有常樂我淨的顛倒想，內心有執著的凡夫，對於顛倒事，如欲取、見取、戒禁取、我語取等堅固執著，忍可認同，為人開示解說邪見，成立顛倒邪見言論，這是見倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、無顛倒2　巳一、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無顛倒，說明想無顛倒的差別，分二科；第一科釋，解釋有智慧的人了知境界無常苦空無我，通達我空、法空的真實義沒有想倒，是無顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無顛倒差別者，謂諸聰叡有所曉了，隨智慧明起如理作意，於所緣境，無常知無常，苦知是苦，不淨知不淨，無我知無我，正取相轉，是名想無顛倒、心無顛倒、見無顛倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無顛倒的差別相，指諸多聰明叡智的有情，通達諸法實相，內心常有智慧的光明，生起如理作意，對於身受心法、有情世間器世間等，於無常如實了知無常，於苦如實了知是苦，於不淨如實了知是不淨，於無我如實了知是無我，能正確取得境相，所以是想無顛倒、心無顛倒、見無顛倒。資糧位及加行位的修行者能隨順無顛倒想，聖人則一切時處不再顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結名無顛倒差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名無顛倒差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有智慧的人如實了知諸法無常、苦、空、無我，不同於凡夫的顛倒想，這是無顛倒想的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、分別2　巳一、辨2　午一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科分別，隨釋想蘊的想分別，分二科；第一科辨，辨識什麼是想分別，又分二科；第一科標列，列出五種想分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4276"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">分別差別者，略有五種想分別相。一、境界分別，二、領納分別，三、假設分別，四、虛妄分別，五、實義分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想有各種的分別差別，要略而言有五種想分別相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、境界分別，執取境相；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、領納分別，執取境界所生受；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、假設分別，於境界執取假名；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、虛妄分別，於境界生顛倒想；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、實義分別，於境界離顛倒想。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、隨釋5　未一、境界分別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，解釋想的五種分別，分五科；第一科境界分別，執境為實而生愛味，名境界分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於境界取隨味相，名境界分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心於所緣境取相生喜生樂，想心所愛樂取著境界，這是境界分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、領納分別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科領納分別，執取境界生受，是領納分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">執取境界所生諸受，名領納分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六根六識觸對境界時，內心隨境生起不同的感受，執取這些差別諸受的分別，是領納分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、假設分別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科假設分別，想依名言取相名假設分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若於自他，取如是名、如是類、如是姓等種種世俗言說相，名假設分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　面對境界時，取著自己及他人的名字、受生的種類、族姓差別等種種世俗言說相，這是假設分別。依事安立的名句文身都是假施設而有的，想依此假名領取境相，稱為假設分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、虛妄分別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科虛妄分別，顛倒想是虛妄分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸境界取顛倒相，名虛妄分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於有為諸境執取常樂我淨的顛倒相，是虛妄分別。凡夫心常是虛妄分別，顛顛倒倒而不自知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、實義分別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科實義分別，無顛倒想是實義分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸境界取無倒相，名實義分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聰明叡智的人通達諸法無我、無實的真實義，對於諸境界不再顛倒取相執著常樂我淨，執著真實，這是實義分別。修學聖道或成就聖道者能有這種分別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結說名想蘊分別差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4277"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是總名想蘊分別差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說包括：想對境愛味生境界分別、執境界生受成領納分別、依名取境成假設分別、顛倒取相成虛妄分別、離顛倒想成實義分別，這些總名為想蘊分別差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、行蘊2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科行蘊，說明行蘊的差別相，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，云何行蘊差別？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，什麼是行蘊的差別相呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出行蘊五種差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亦由五相。一、由境界故；二、由分位故；三、由雜染故；四、由清淨故；五、由造作故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行蘊也有五種相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由境界，建立眼等六觸生思：六思身；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由分位，建立生等二十四不相應行；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由雜染，建立根本煩惱及隨煩惱；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、由清淨，建立信等十一種善心所；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由造作，建立為境隨與等五種造作相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋5　辰一、由境界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，隨釋行蘊的差別相，分五科；第一科由境界，依根境識和合而安立六觸所生思的六思身。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由境界者，謂於行蘊立六思身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由境界者，是指於行蘊安立六思身。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六識生時同時有作意、觸、受、想、思五遍行心所，除受、想心所以外，思心所及其餘的心所都屬於行蘊所攝，若依境界安立行蘊則別指六觸生思的六思身。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、由分位</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由分位，由行蘊的分位差別，及身心的變化，安立生老住無常等二十四不相應行的行蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由分位者，謂立生等不相應行，由彼生等唯有分位所顯現故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由分位是指依身心分位變化的差異，而安立生、老、住、無常等二十四不相應行法，這都是屬於行蘊所攝。由生、老、住、無常等而顯現身心分位的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、由雜染</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由雜染，說明行蘊的雜染差別，依內心雜染建立煩惱的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由雜染者，謂於雜染諸行建立煩惱及隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　雜染是指內心有煩惱的染污。由煩惱雜染的活動，而建立煩惱的差別，有貪瞋癡慢見疑等六種根本煩惱，不信、懈怠、放逸、惛沈、掉舉、失念、不正知、散亂的八大隨煩惱，無慚、無愧的二中隨煩惱，及忿、恨、惱、覆、誑、諂、憍、害、嫉、慳十小隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、由清淨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由清淨，說明依內心清淨於行蘊建立信等十一種善心所。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="53p4278"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由清淨者，謂於清淨諸行建立信等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了成就聖道清淨內心，而建立行蘊的清淨差別，有信、勤、慚、愧、無貪、無瞋、無癡、輕安、不放逸、行捨、不害十一個善心所。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、由造作</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科由造作，由造作的差別，有五種相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由造作者，謂如前說五造作相，為境隨與等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依行蘊造作的差別，而安立五種行蘊的造作相，包括為境隨與等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》為境隨與等者：前說五造作相。一、為境隨與，二、為彼合會，三、為彼別離，四、能發雜染業，五、令心自在轉。此應準知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前文說行有五種造作相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、為境隨與，由思心所推動心去隨順參與境界，於可意境思欲和合，於不可意境思欲別離；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、為彼合會，由思的造作推動內心與可愛境合會；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、為彼別離，由思的造作推動內心遠離不可愛境；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、能發雜染業，由於有煩惱而不如理作意，而發動身三口四意三等十不善業；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、令心自在轉，透過修學禪定及聖道，有如理作意及勝解心所等和合，而令心遠離煩惱自在而轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五十三</span></strong></span></span><br />
&nbsp;</p>
